Yan's Arrangements Before Leaving Shanxi

Xu Yongchang to Oversee the Aftermath

Yan Xishan Lavishly Rewards Subordinates

Taiyuan dispatch: After the return of Wen Shouquan and Liang Ruzhou from Liaoning, Yan Xishan, considering the deteriorating environment, had already completed preparations in Wutai and decided to go abroad. It is expected that he will depart within the month. Yan is currently residing in Jian'an Village, where Feng Yuxiang previously resided last year. High-ranking military and political figures have been flocking to pay their respects. After Yan leaves the province, Xu Yongchang, under the title of Garrison Commander of Shanxi and Suiyuan, will temporarily be responsible for maintaining order in Shanxi in conjunction with Provincial Chairman Shang Zhen. Xu is scheduled to take office on the 18th. According to general observations, Xu's appointment is purely transitional, and the real solutions will await the decision of the central government. Fu Zuoyi has recently been appointed by Yan as the Garrison Commander of the Peiping-Suiyuan Railway and went to Datong to assume office yesterday. Feng Yuxiang's whereabouts are now rumored to be in Fenyang, and there are even rumors that Yan will go there to meet him, but it is not confirmed. To reward his subordinates before leaving the country, Yan withdrew seven million yuan in cash from the Provincial Bank. Military officers above the rank of brigade commander and civilian officials who were Yan's confidants were each given rewards ranging from five thousand to fifteen thousand yuan. According to internal sources from the Provincial Bank, when Yan returned to Taiyuan from Shizhuang, the bank still had more than 13 million yuan in cash. After Yan withdrew 7 million yuan, spent 2 to 3 million yuan on miscellaneous expenses and refunded 20% of the share capital, the bank now has only about 3 million yuan. According to official announcements, the total amount of banknotes issued by the Provincial Bank is 47.5 million yuan. After Yan leaves Shanxi, leaving behind only this worthless paper, the lives of the 13 million people in the province are uncertain. This is indeed a major problem currently facing Shanxi. Since Liang Ruzhou's return to Taiyuan, Yan's headquarters convened a meeting of all staff the day before yesterday, ordering the completion of all preparations within three days. The public meals provided there will be canceled tomorrow. In recent days, communist saboteurs have been repeatedly arrested in Taiyuan, and officials have implemented unusually strict security measures in the city. Curfews are enforced every night at 11:00 PM. Former provincial party members are still secretly plotting and actively engaging in activities. (November 17th)

Japanese Garrison in Fengcheng, Liaoning, Kills Chinese Again

Two Murders in Three Months

Shenyang dispatch: Another incident of the Japanese garrison killing Chinese has occurred in Fengcheng County, Liaoning Province. Previously, there was an incident where the Japanese garrison brutally killed Chinese, which was repeatedly protested but yielded no results. Now, there has been another shooting of Chinese. Initially, Liu Decai, a farmer from Xigou Village, Fengcheng, in his thirties, with a wife, Liu Wangshi, and children, was a hired worker at the home of Ai Shuquan in Aijiabaozi. On the afternoon of the 14th of this month, at 7:00 PM, Liu was returning home to get clothes when he encountered a Japanese garrison patrol by the railway. They immediately subjected him to inspection. There were no other people at the time. For some unknown reason, they stabbed Liu several times with bayonets. Liu screamed for help in extreme pain. Although nearby residents heard the cries, no one dared to help due to the usual intimidating power of the Japanese garrison. Finally, Liu was shot and killed by the Japanese garrison. The next day, Chen Fangxiang, the village chief of Xigou, reported it to the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau. After verification by Branch Chief Ao Shizhang, the incident was reported to the county government. The county government sent personnel to the scene of the incident with the Japanese garrison for inspection. They found the deceased lying face up on the road, with blood stains blurred, a tragic sight. The inspection revealed one bayonet wound on the outside of the deceased's right arm, two bayonet wounds under the right armpit, one bayonet wound on the back, and one bullet wound on the left side of the ribs, proving that he was first stabbed with a knife and then shot to death. The deceased's wife, Liu Wangshi, and their two children cried loudly when they saw the scene, requesting the county government to seek justice for the deceased. The county government made a reasoned protest to the Japanese side. The Japanese garrison claimed that they were patrolling the area at 7:30 PM that night and saw Liu moving a large stone onto the tracks. They intended to arrest him, but Liu resisted with a wooden stick, causing accidental injury, etc. The county government said that regardless of whether the farmer had unlawful behavior, even if he did, how could a small wooden stick resist sharp firearms? Who can believe this situation? Later, the county government comforted the family of the deceased and temporarily buried the deceased, reporting the situation to the provincial government and instructing the Foreign Affairs Office to lodge a serious protest with the Japanese side. The Liaoning National Foreign Affairs Association was extremely indignant about this case, stating that there have been two cases of the Japanese garrison in Fengcheng shooting and killing Chinese within three months, treating the lives of our people like dirt, with extreme animosity. How can our people rest easy? The association is now appealing to the authorities to seek justice for the deceased. (November 21st)

Closing of the Belgian Exposition

Chinese Exhibits Win Third Prize

Liège dispatch: The Belgian Centennial Exposition, which opened on May 3rd, attracted tens of thousands of visitors from various countries daily. Except for the educational and agricultural exhibits, which were primarily for display, most of the industrial and commercial exhibits from China have been sold, especially tea, silk, porcelain, cloisonné, carpets, and embroidery, which were very popular with foreigners. The awards ceremony was held in October. The Belgian King and cabinet members attended, as well as diplomatic corps and representatives from various countries. Chinese representative Chu Minyi, Deputy Representative Liu Xichang, and Chargé d'Affaires Xie Shou Kang participated. According to the announcement of the award results by the Belgian government's on-site supervisor, a total of more than 3,600 awards were given throughout the event. France won first place, Belgium second, and China third, accounting for nearly one-tenth of the total awards at the event, totaling more than 300. Since the six-month period has expired, the event is scheduled to close on November 3rd. A farewell banquet was held on October 27th in the Liège Provincial Government, chaired by the Provincial Governor. Representatives from various countries attended the ceremony. Since Chinese representative Chu Minyi had departed from the United States to return to China, Deputy Representative Liu Xichang attended. A total of more than 200 foreign guests attended the conference. The Governor of Liège delivered a speech first, mainly thanking the representatives of various countries, expressing satisfaction with the excellent results of this exposition, and all the people of various countries were very satisfied. Afterwards, the representatives of various countries jointly elected the French representative to deliver a reply. During the banquet, many dancers held social dances, accompanied by music, and the banquet dispersed late at night. The exposition has now closed, and the Chinese affairs closing matters were handled by Deputy Representative Liu Xichang with Secretary Tian Shoucheng. Now, it is known that all matters have been settled, and there are more than fifty boxes of exhibits shipped back to China. Mr. Liu and others left Belgium on November 13th and returned to China via Siberia.

Domestic News 2

Hunan Province Mobilizes for Bandit Suppression

He Jian Exhorts His Troops to Strive to Suppress the Communists

Changsha dispatch: Hunan Province has recently implemented bandit suppression, but the bandit forces have not yet been quelled. For example, the scattered bandits in Nanhua have not been cleared, the siege of Jinfeng has been lifted, but He Long and Kuang Jixun have captured Cishi, advancing towards Changtao. This is the situation in western Hunan. Pingjiang and Liuyang counties have fallen entirely into red influence. Communist leaders Kong Helong, Hu Jun, Zhang Jingwu, and others have been entrenched in Pingjiang and Liuyang for more than a month, engaging in dozens of battles with government forces, and the bandit forces remain the same. Kong's bandits even broke out of Pingjiang, Changle, and Xinshi, rushing into Miluo, destroying the railway, cutting off transportation between Hunan and Hubei, and this has happened twice. Each time, it took several days or more than ten days of effort to repel them. At present, the county seat of Pingjiang is still in the hands of the bandits. Although the county seat of Liuyang is in the hands of the government forces, the communist forces are in all rural areas and still need to be cleared. This is the situation in Pingjiang and Liuyang. Anren and Chaling counties have been captured twice in a month by Chen Shao's bandit troops, and all the militia guns have been confiscated. A few days ago, Duan Heng, the commander of the Southern Hunan Garrison, led his troops to recover them, but Chen's bandits are still entrenched in Lianhua, Jiangxi, and there is a possibility of frequent incursions. In addition, the communists in Ji'an are also threatening to flee to Chaling. The people of eastern Hunan are fleeing to the province one after another. Seeing this situation, He Jian knows that nothing can be done without a painful suppression, so he assembled his troops and concentrated them in separate ways, completing the concentration before the 19th of this month, and launching a general attack in separate ways at the same time on the morning of the 20th. The plan and troop allocation are as follows: (1) In western Hunan, Ma Kunshan's division of the Sichuan Army, totaling three regiments, will suppress Jinfeng and clear the scattered bandits. Zhang Ying's division of the Sichuan Army, totaling three regiments, and Cheng Tiexia's brigade of the 16th Hunan Army, totaling two regiments, will clear the scattered bandits in Nanhua. In addition, Chen Quzhen's six regiments of the First Garrison Command and Dai Huiheng's three regiments of the Western Hunan Bandit Suppression Command will be the pursuit troops, surrounding Cishi and pursuing He and Kuang's bandits. (2) In Pingjiang and Liuyang, Tao Guang's 31st Division, totaling four regiments, Wang Dongyuan's 15th Division, totaling six regiments, and Zhu Xingyu's Bandit Suppression Second Battalion, totaling eleven regiments, will attack the county seat of Pingjiang, and send Liu Jianxu, the commander of the 28th Army, to supervise the battle in Zhushayu Qianzhan, first clearing Pingjiang, and then pursuing Jiangxi Tonggu and Xiushui. Liuyang will be cleared by Chen Guangzhong's Fourth Regiment of the Independent Seventh Brigade, Bai Shinuo's One Regiment of the Security Corps, and the West Liuyang Volunteer Team, searching and advancing towards Gugang Dongmen City, first clearing Liuyang, and then pursuing Jiangxi Wanzai. In addition, Tong Kun's two regiments of the Second Bandit Suppression Brigade in western Hunan, Guo Bugao's One Battalion of the First Bandit Suppression Battalion, and Ye Wenke's Independent Regiment of the General Headquarters will be deployed between Yuezhou and Xiangyin Miluo to protect the road and prevent the communist bandits in Pingjiang from rushing out to destroy the road, and Gu Weiren, the commander of the 16th Division, will be stationed in Miluo to command. (3) In eastern Hunan, Duan Heng's two regiments of the Southern Hunan Garrison Command and Li Jue's four regiments of the 19th Division will search and advance towards Lianhua Fenyi from Chaling. The above-mentioned mobilization force totaled 43 regiments, approximately 56,000 people, who were all dispatched at the same time on the 20th to suppress the bandits in separate ways. On the evening of the 20th, Army Commander Liu Jianxu sent a telegram from the front line of Zhushayu, saying that Wang Dongyuan attacked Pingcheng from Daqiaoyu Sanyangjie Lusu Mountain at dawn, Tao Guang's division attacked Pingcheng from Sanjiaotang Chengtan, and Zhu Xingyu's battalion attacked Pingcheng from Jinjiashi Tianyue Mountain. Nearly 10,000 bandits stubbornly resisted, holding out until 4:00 PM. Tao Guang's Zhong Guangren Brigade broke through the bandit troops and broke into Pingcheng, killing many bandits. He was following Tao's division to advance towards Pingcheng, and most of the bandits fled to Nanjiang. Also, Brigade Commander Chen Guangzhong telegraphed that the bandit nest in Shihuhas been broken, killing more than 100 bandits and capturing 20 alive, and is now pursuing Mianchong. There has been progress in Pingjiang and Liuyang. The situation in other areas has not yet been reported. Before the mobilization, in order to boost morale, He Jian specially requested Commander-in-Chief Chiang to promote Chen Guangzhong, who was effective in suppressing bandits, to the commander of the 32nd Division, Dai Huiheng to the commander of the Independent Seventh Brigade, Li Muming (originally the chief of staff and second brigade commander of Chen Guangzhong's division) to the commander of the Independent Eighth Brigade, and Tong Kun to the commander of the Independent Ninth Brigade. He also sent a telegram to all his officers and men, earnestly exhorting them to strive to suppress the communists. The text of the telegram is as follows: "It has been found that the communist bandits led by Zhu, Mao, Peng, Huang, He, Kuang, Kong, and Li have been harming the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi for several years, killing and setting fires, doing everything. To sum up their crimes, it is heartbreaking. Previously, they have been repeatedly suppressed, but the bandits are cunning and evasive, and have not been wiped out. Now our army has been ordered to cooperate with the friendly armies of the three provinces to suppress the bandits. All the deployment of troops and pursuit plans have been issued for compliance. This suppression of bandits is directly to relieve the people of their suffering, and indirectly to lay the foundation of the party and the country on a solid foundation. It is especially important to the military prestige and reputation of our army. Now that the communist bandits are no longer as concentrated as before, and we have made sufficient preparations, the outcome of the victory or defeat is certain. If we still miss the opportunity and do not make a permanent plan, then the opportunity will be lost and the disaster will be great in the future, and the future will be uncertain, and we will not know where to die. Our officers and soldiers have always been loyal to the party and the country and have made meritorious service. We hope to inspire our conscience and strive to kill the thieves. We should all have the determination that if there are communists, there will be no us, and if there is us, there will be no communists. We should fight the bandits immediately without hesitation. In particular, we should not stand in a passive position, but should seek out the main force of the bandits, track and painfully suppress them, and destroy them all in one fell swoop. As for punishing those who follow the bandits and capturing the bandit masses, indiscriminate killing is useless, and indulgence is also impossible. It is important to use heavy punishment to govern the chaos. It is hoped that the army commanders and commanders will understand this purpose. All the security in the rear has been planned, so there is no need to worry. The responsibility belongs to you, so don't worry about it. There will be generous rewards for meritorious service in killing thieves, and those who are ineffective in battle will be punished according to the law. We hope that we will all work together. This is the most important thing." (November 21st)

Organizational Structure of Liang Guanying's Troops

Xuzhou dispatch: Liang Guanying's 25th Route Army is being transferred to northern Jiangsu, under the command of Zhang Zhijiang, and has already begun its march. Liang's general headquarters is located in Qingjiangpu. The organizational structure of the troops in Henan has already been completed. The newly designated numbers include the 32nd Division, attached with the Independent 5th Brigade and four independent regiments. Officers at all levels have also been appointed. Liang concurrently serves as the commander of the 32nd Division, with Dai, Pan, and Zhou as his deputies. The division is divided into three brigades: Zhao Jianxun as the commander of the 94th Brigade, commanding Pan Taowan's, Li Qinhu's, and Shi Faxue's three regiments; Liu Guoming as the commander of the 95th Brigade, commanding Jiang Xiuren's, Cao Dianwen's, and Wang Fanhong's three regiments; Wang Xiushen as the commander of the 96th Brigade, commanding Xia Wenzhang's, Chen Maolin's, and Wen Zongyu's three regiments. In addition, Zheng Tingzhen is the commander of the Independent 5th Brigade, Gao Guojun is the commander of the Special Service Regiment, Zeng Jirui is the commander of the Pistol Regiment, Li Ruixuan is the commander of the Artillery Regiment, and Wang Ligong is the commander of the Cavalry Regiment. The organization of the general headquarters has also been completed, with Li Yuanhui as the chief of staff, divided into eight sections: Cheng Peng, chief of the staff section; Xi Qiran, chief of the adjutant section; Guo Hongxun, chief of the quartermaster section; Mei Daozhou, chief of the military law section; Yang Cunyi, chief of the medical section; Li Yanbang, chief of the ordnance section; Wu Fengzhang, chief of the military affairs section; and Li Zhimin, director of the secretarial section. Currently, the 94th and 96th brigades have arrived in northern Jiangsu. The Independent 5th Brigade and the four independent regiments are being transported. The 95th Brigade and the headquarters will be the last to depart for Qingjiangpu. Liu Zhenbang, director of the quartermaster section of the 32nd Division, and Gao Shixuan, quartermaster of the Independent 5th Brigade, are currently handling food supplies in Xuzhou. There are reports that Li Yunheng's troops will take over the defense of Guide. (November 24th)

Four-Way Vehicle Clearing Meeting

Xuzhou dispatch: The four-way vehicle clearing meeting of the Jinpu, Jiaoji, Longhai, and Pinghan railways was held at the Xuzhou Garden Hotel on the 17th of this month. The representatives of each road attended the meeting. The Jinpu Railway representatives were She Xu, Zhang Fan, Zhong Guidan, Zhao Keng, and Cheng Gui; the Jiaoji Railway representatives were Su Bubin, Yang Heng, Cao Yi, and Cao Changqi; the Longhai Railway representatives were Xiao Xinwu and Xu Zhongwei; the Pinghan Railway representative was Jin Yuanxun; and the Transportation Headquarters representative was Huang Xuezhou. The Ministry of Railways sent three staff members, Xu Chuanyin, Li Yue, and Tang Dehua. Qian Zongze, the commander of the transportation, presided over the meeting and reported on the military transportation operations of the Ministry of Transportation from its establishment on the 23rd to its dissolution on November 15th, the inter-transfer of vehicles, and the efforts to maintain them. Among them, the Jinpu and Longhai railways had the most vehicles crossing each other's tracks, and the Jiaoji and Pinghan railways had fewer. Therefore, the clearing was mainly focused on the Jinpu and Longhai railways, which were more complicated. The Jiaoji and Pinghan railways had less to do with it. After the report, Xu Chuanyin, the staff member of the Ministry of Railways, continued to preside over the meeting. The most important issue to be resolved in the morning meeting was to clear the vehicles crossing the tracks. It was agreed that Ni Peizhi would be sent by the Jinpu Railway, Zhang Hongyan by the Longhai Railway, Cao Yi by the Jiaoji Railway, and He Rongdi by the Pinghan Railway to be responsible for investigating the vehicle numbers for clearing. The standard for clearing was also determined, based on the signatures of the stationmasters on both sides of the track. All vehicles that crossed the tracks during the military transportation period and were not returned would be returned unconditionally. For those that exceeded the military period, they would be returned according to tonnage. According to the recent investigation results, the Jiaoji Railway had approximately 100 vehicles stranded on other routes, which need to be calculated with the Jinpu Railway in Jinan. The Pinghan Railway was barely able to cope, and the entire route had not been unified, so it was difficult to clear for the time being. The clearing situation of the Jinpu and Longhai railways: during the military period, the Longhai Railway delivered 529 passenger cars and 1,440 freight cars to the Jinpu Railway, totaling 369,467 tons. The Jinpu Railway delivered 484 passenger cars and 14,373 freight cars to the Longhai Railway, totaling 368,702 tons. The difference between the two is 45 passenger cars, 34 freight cars, totaling 765 tons. The clearing is roughly like this, but the opinions on the clearing plan of each route do not seem to be consistent. She Xu, the representative of the Jinpu Railway, has already returned to Pukou yesterday to report and ask for instructions. Therefore, the meeting has not been able to completely solve the clearing of vehicles. (November 24th)

Xietang Huimin Bridge Completed: The Xietang Huimin Bridge in the county is a huge project. It has been under construction since the beginning of autumn and was finally completed the other day. Gao Ying's Soil Transportation Case to be Retried: Gao Ying and Sun Yuan's soil transportation case has been returned to the High Court for retrial this time. The High Court stated that Gao Ying claimed that he did not receive a telegram from his wife Liao to go to the wharf to meet him on that day, but went to pick up Chinese workers to land. Therefore, it sent an official letter to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the National Government for investigation. Yesterday, the High Court received a reply from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, stating that Gao Ying did go to the wharf on that day to pick up Chinese workers to land. After receiving the reply, the High Court determined that the points that needed to be investigated in the case had been successively investigated and returned to the court, so it decided to open the trial in the near future.

Summary of County Government Meeting

The County Government held its 73rd county administration meeting on the 24th. The following important matters were resolved: (1) The expenses for each district to hold township head and autonomous staff elections will be allocated by the county government, with the Finance Bureau instructed to transfer funds from local sources. An average of four yuan per township will be budgeted, with each district head responsible for managing the funds frugally. Any shortfall will be made up by the district office. (2) The County Education Bureau's request to allocate the county's retained overdue fines for education expenses, now ordered to be remitted to the province, should be compensated by the county from other sources and submitted for discussion at the third county administrative meeting. (3) During the winter defense period, the local importance of the towns of Gelong and Qianmentang should be emphasized. The county government will request that the Construction Department quickly approve the long-distance telephone plans for these two towns, which are part of the bureau’s planned second phase of long-distance telephone construction, and promptly issue installation fees of one thousand yuan to facilitate immediate installation for defense purposes.

More Bandits Arrested in Shanghai in Connection with Robbery and Kidnapping Case

常州

Tragic Vendetta Case Occurs at Haizhekou

At Haizhekou, west of Wuyi City, four men, Liu Dexi, Liu Zhanen, Lü Dejun, and Lü Fengdong, suddenly arrived at the Juchang and Changmaosheng lumber yards on the evening of the 23rd. They fired a shot first and then entered the Juchang lumber yard. There, they stabbed the night watchman, Chen Zhaoqi, in the throat and waist, causing him to bleed from the kidneys and fall supine on the ground. They then went to the Changmaosheng lumber yard and stabbed the night watchman, Kang Youli, in the head and throat, causing him to immediately fall to the ground and die. Kang Youlin and Yu Shan were also stabbed and injured. The next morning, the incident was reported to the nearby Public Security First Branch and Second Substation, which sent officers to investigate and confirmed the facts. In addition to the injured being taken to Wujin Hospital for treatment by the people in charge, Patrol Officer Xu Chizhi also prepared a document to be submitted to the Public Security Bureau to cooperate in arresting the perpetrators and bringing them to justice. Furthermore, according to news this (25th) morning, the injured Chen Zhaoqi has died from his injuries at Wujin Hospital.

Yan Junnan's Case Adjourned for Trial

Yan Junnan, the former captain of the county police brigade, was corrupt and unlawful, losing over a hundred firearms in Siyu. The eighteen district heads of the entire county reported this to the province, and the Provincial Bandit Suppression Headquarters detained and interrogated him, summoning the district heads to testify. Due to the short notice, the county requested an adjournment, which was approved. The complainants are ordered to appear for interrogation in two weeks to conclude the case.

Joint Suppression of Haian Port Pirates

The Daian Port at the junction of Tonghai has recently become a base for pirates. The water and land police teams are attacking, but the bandits are stubbornly resisting in the shallow waters. The county government has telegraphed the Navy to dispatch seaplanes to assist in the suppression.

Page 10

常熟

Another Kidnapping Case Occurs in Xiyang Town

Six people, including Zhang Chengqi, a traditional Chinese medicine practitioner in Xiyang Town, Fushan District of this county, were kidnapped by bandits last month and are still missing. Unexpectedly, the other night (the 22nd) around 10 p.m., over fifty pirates, traveling in five civilian boats, arrived in the town. Each carried weapons. When they first arrived at the port, there happened to be an anti-smuggling patrol boat docked there. The pirates immediately surrounded the patrol boat. The police, outnumbered, had all their firearms seized, including one rifle, two Mauser pistols, and one carbine. After seizing the weapons, they rushed into the home of Bang Youchong and looted it, stealing over a hundred silver dollars and jewelry. Before leaving, they kidnapped You Heng's son, Tian Chen, his sister-in-law, Zhu, and his niece, Gui Jian. They then went to the home of Wang Bosheng in the same neighborhood and kidnapped his son, Gui, and his niece, Zhao Mei. It is said that Zhou Youheng was previously kidnapped by bandits and paid a ransom of 30,000 yuan to secure his release. He had barely escaped danger when his son was kidnapped again. It is said that his suffering is unbearable.

鎭江

Money Industry Sends Representatives to Shanghai to Arrange for Accounting Period

The Zhenjiang business community feels inconvenienced by the initial adoption of the Gregorian calendar for settling accounts this year. The Chamber of Commerce and the Money Industry Association have discussed this repeatedly. They agree that Shanghai is the commercial center of the country and that they must follow its lead and proceed step by step, slightly modifying their practices when necessary. Yesterday, the Money Industry Association publicly appointed Hu Jingxuan and Sheng Pengji to travel to Shanghai immediately, carrying official letters, to directly consult with the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce for solutions.

Ding Fengxiang Silk Mill Closes Again Yesterday

The Zhenjiang Ding Fengxiang Silk Mill, currently managed by Miao Shaoqing, a cocoon merchant from Wuxi, and renamed Yingyu Company, resumed operations the other day (the 23rd). Unexpectedly, after only one day of operation, it announced another shutdown yesterday (the 24th). The reason is said to be that when the mill was reopened, it only had fifteen bales of silk cocoons transported from Wuxi. The remaining cocoons were to be transported to Zhenjiang after operations resumed. Unexpectedly, the cocoons were detained at the Wuxi station by a group of female workers in Wuxi, making it impossible to continue operations. Mr. Miao, upon hearing this news, went to Wuxi to negotiate with them.

揚州

Education Bureau Chief Trapped

The Education Bureau of Yangzhong County has six or seven hundred acres of school land located in Beisha, which belongs to Taixing County. However, it is all along the river embankment, and the tidal flats are unstable. Since Feng Zidan, a sand bully from that area, reported claiming over two hundred acres to the Taixing Sand Field Bureau, the boundary lines have been unclear, leading to lawsuits since the 15th year of the Republic. Although there has been a land survey, the Taixing side has not thoroughly resolved the issue, allowing the dispute to continue, resulting in a pending case. Now that the time for cutting reeds is approaching, the Yangzhong County Education Bureau specifically requested and was approved by County Magistrate Xu to issue a joint public notice with County Magistrate Ma of Taixing, prohibiting cutting until the matter is resolved. This public notice was taken by Wang Huankun, the Director of the Education Bureau of Yangzhong, to be posted. Unexpectedly, Feng Zidan's side had already received the news. When Director Wang arrived at the sandbar, they immediately summoned over a hundred people to prevent the posting and trapped Director Wang, demanding and threatening him, while they themselves cut the reeds. Fortunately, a carter returned to the bureau to report. Upon receiving the news, the Education Bureau reported to the 21st Squad of the Fifth District of the Water Police, requesting them to send police to suppress the situation and seal off the cut reeds. It is expected that Director Wang will be able to escape danger and return to the bureau within a few days.

Suddenly Arrested While Attending a Wedding

Yao De Gui, a villager residing in Yaojia Tan Village behind Xinglong Town, was previously arrested for a kidnapping case. After being released, he returned to farming. On the 22nd of this month, there was a wedding in a neighboring village, and De Gui went to offer congratulations and help. Unexpectedly, while he was enjoying the wedding banquet, he was suddenly arrested by a bailiff from the county government. He was bound with hemp rope and taken to Sanmao Town, escorted to the county government, and taken into custody. All those attending the wedding banquet were baffled. It is said that the reason for the arrest was due to the villager's previous appeal to the provincial government after being released, but it is not known for certain.

淸江

A Singular Fire Accident

Outside the East Gate of Huaiyin County, there used to be one large and one small City God Temple. The large City God Temple was south of the Grand Canal, and the small City God Temple was north of the canal. Every year on the tenth day of the tenth month of the lunar calendar, superstitious men and women would go to the temples to burn incense. The burning of incense was more popular than in any other temple in the county. Yesterday, on the tenth day of the tenth lunar month, superstitious men and women from various places again went to burn incense and pray for blessings. Unexpectedly, the monks in both temples disregarded the ban and did not dare to openly come out to greet the worshippers, resulting in fires in both temples. The losses were especially heavy in the large City God Temple, with one main hall and several wooden puppets burned down. The cause of the fires was the unextinguished incense candles, which is quite strange.

Wei San's Bandit Gang Flees to Anhui

Wei San's bandit gang, which had been entrenched in the Jinjia and Caojia Temple area in the western countryside of Siyang, had seven or eight hundred followers. Since last winter, for nearly a year, this gang of bandits has roamed around, robbing, looting, burning, and killing, without restraint. The people of Siyang were most pained by this. Since the Jiangsu Provincial Waterborne Public Security Team arrived in Siyang last month, they have joined forces with the county police and militia to strike hard, causing Wei San's gang to suffer many casualties. Moreover, they have also split into several smaller groups and no longer dare to confront the government troops. According to people from Siyang who came to Pu, the various small groups of bandits that have split off have completely retreated to Suxian and other places in northern Anhui, no longer remaining in western Siyang. As a result, the Xia Lingyun unit, the Second Battalion of the 266th Regiment, which had previously been dispatched to Siyang, also returned to Puyuan this afternoon (the 22nd) for rest.

平湖

Bandit News in Yaqian Township

At the beginning of this month, the family of Miao Wuxiang in Jiuyafang, west of Yaqian District, received a threatening letter from bandits demanding 2,000 silver dollars. Miao ignored it. The bandits came repeatedly to demand payment, but Wuxiang avoided meeting them. On the 17th, six bandits returned to his home, carrying bundles of firewood and piling them around the house, claiming that if he did not pay, they would burn the house down on the spot. Wuxiang had no choice but to ask the laity monk to negotiate, agreeing to pay 500 silver dollars to settle the matter.

Kidnapping Case in Beifang Port

At 11:00 p.m. on the night of the 21st, the home of Gu Liuxiang in Beifang Port, east of town, was robbed. Clothes, silver dollars, and rice were all looted. The bandits kidnapped two of Liuxiang's sons, both young and old. The Gu family was robbed once during the summer. This time, they suffered another looting, and their two sons were kidnapped, which can be described as a double misfortune.

杭州

Preparing to Abolish Likin and Investigate Businesses

The Zhejiang Provincial Department of Finance believes that the central government is actively moving towards the abolition of likin, and Jiangsu Province has already implemented business tax. Zhejiang Province should not delay preparations for business tax. However, the business conditions in this province vary between eastern and western Zhejiang, making it difficult to unify. The tax rates should not be divided and other issues. Therefore, it has started formulating various business condition survey forms yesterday in order to dispatch personnel to investigate everything immediately.

Increasing Funds for Second and Third Class Counties

The Zhejiang Provincial Government, based on a proposal by Cheng Zhenjun, the acting head of the Department of Civil Affairs, plans to complete the organization law of all counties in the province in the 19th year of the Republic. In addition to the fourteen counties that have already been reorganized, the others should be organized according to laws and regulations to achieve completion. During the budget meeting, the administrative expenses of second and third class counties will be increased by 200 yuan each to facilitate the process. The department has now set December 1st as the implementation date.

蕭山

Prohibiting Farmers' Associations from Privately Collecting Land Tax

In Xiaoshan, Xizhou, Konghu, and other villages, some illegal farmers, such as Zhang Huanying, have been privately collecting land tax of 30 or 35 cents per mu. If there is no money, it is replaced with items. It is found that there are more than 3,000 mu of land contracts in each village, totaling 18,000 mu in six villages. Collecting a tax of 35 cents is a considerable amount. Both tenants and landlords are being exploited. Citizens such as Shi Fengyi have petitioned the county to request a public notice strictly prohibiting farmers' associations from illegally collecting taxes. County Magistrate Du issued a strict prohibition after receiving the petition. Anyone who commits such acts in the future will be severely investigated according to the law.

Letter Received

Letter from Cui Siping, Chief of the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau of Jiangyin County

Dear Sir, I recently read an item in the Local News column of your newspaper (24th) stating that a hawker from Jiangyin was detained and fined by our branch and then released, which does not correspond with the facts. According to our records, on the evening of the 19th of this month, our bureau learned that gambling was taking place at the Ge residence in Hexi. The bureau chief immediately led police to arrest the gamblers, capturing four people, including Ge Laosi and others. Upon investigation, it was a small mahjong game, so they were sentenced to ten days detention each in accordance with Article 45 of the Law on Punishment of Violations of Police Regulations to serve as a warning. No fines were imposed afterwards. These are the established facts. Furthermore, the county government and the Public Security Bureau of this county have not revoked the investigation. It seems that your reporter stationed in Cheng County heard an inaccurate rumor. I am specially informing you of the detailed and accurate situation and request that you make a correction to clarify the truth. Sincerely, Cui Siping, Chief of the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau of Jiangyin County, November 24th.

Free Talk

A Word of Wisdom

— Yimei

As the sun sets, so desolate is the solitary figure. This situation is most unbearable.

The deepest impression in my mind, the one that is not easily erased, is the shallow smile of that person.

True beauty does not require powder. True writing does not require embellishment.

A pot of chrysanthemums placed in a small study has its own unique charm. If one gathers hundreds or thousands of varieties and stacks them into a mountain, it will only be confusing and uninteresting.

Most domestic films depict bandit dens and thief gangs, no different from showing foreigners that our country's society is a combination of thieves.

When a person becomes rich and noble, they lose their warmth. Mackerel loses its flavor. A mansion loses its shelter. A wife loses her virtue.

Living in the bustling city, disturbed by the dust, I often think of the joy of appreciating the rain in a thatched cottage, surrounded by tall bamboos. Although I do not hope for extravagance, it is still difficult to fulfill my desire.

Better to suffer a loss than to lose honesty and kindness.

Wormwood cannot coexist with orchids. If wormwood flourishes, the orchids will be destroyed.

One river, one mountain is enough for me to live and die. One flower, one grass is enough to please my heart when I am free and comfort me when I am busy.

Even a few words from a talented person have their own charm. Compared to the lengthy arguments of ordinary people, they only show their effort without any reward.

If money is used properly, it is like a strong man crushing the weak, where one can equal a hundred or a hundred can equal a thousand.

If we writers create a beneficial article every day, then this day cannot be considered wasted.

Cities sometimes have fashionable women, but no good flowers. The countryside has good flowers, but no fashionable women. It is always difficult to have it all.

I am most ashamed when people ask me my age, because I have not cultivated virtue, have not completed my studies, and have not established my career. Suddenly, more than thirty springs and autumns have passed.

A Strange Disease

— Gong Yu

The world is vast and full of wonders. Everything imaginable, no matter how bizarre, exists in the world. Sometimes it even exceeds imagination. Therefore, although the Journey to the West is a Taoist book filled with allegories, since it is imaginable, why shouldn't there be such a powerful stone monkey in the world? Here is a record of a strange disease that is beyond human imagination and yet actually exists. The patient is an eighty-year-old woman, surnamed Xu. Her husband is still alive. Her son is named Sheng Bao. She lives in Xizhuang, north of Xitang City in Changshu. Initially, the old woman had been ill for nearly ten years, lying on her bed, and no medicine was effective. Her husband and son both thought that she was old and had no hope of recovery, so it was useless to waste money on medicine. Unexpectedly, this year, the old woman suddenly recovered and walked as usual, without any signs of senility. The whole family was delighted. When they saw that the old woman was no longer ill but had regained her vitality, her spirit and physique were actually healthier than those of a strong woman, able to climb on beams and roofs, agile beyond comparison, as if she possessed the art of qinggong (light body technique), so they were greatly surprised. She had lost a common illness only to suffer a very unusual one. Since the old woman suffered from this strange disease, her words and actions have been abnormal. The strangest thing is that the old woman constantly shouts, "I want to eat liver!" Sometimes she says "beef liver" or "lamb liver." Although her family considers it delirium, they observe that her condition seems to be that of someone extremely hungry and asking for food, not just senseless babbling. When given ordinary food, she refuses to accept it, shouting to eat liver without end. Soon after, some families nearby had cattle and sheep die of illness. When they were skinned and butchered, their livers were all missing. They couldn't help but exclaim in amazement, believing that the beef and lamb livers were actually eaten by the old woman. But the old woman never goes out, so what method does she use to obtain the beef and lamb livers? Or is it just a coincidence of delirium? This matter spread far and wide. Timid neighbors were worried that the old woman could kill people, and repeatedly warned the old woman's husband and son, advising them to kill the old woman to eliminate the harm to the community. The husband and son were also very frightened, but they hesitated to carry out the deadly act that was recommended by their neighbors. It wasn’t long before the neighbors' imagined fears were realized. A woman surnamed Mou had been bedridden for months. Medicine was ineffective, and her condition worsened over time until she could not get up. The night before, when the woman was in a coma, she suddenly screamed, "Old woman Xu is here! She is eating my liver on the bed! It hurts!" Her voice was shrill, and her face changed with the sound. Her family was terrified and gathered around the bed, holding lamps and illuminating everything. At first, there were no traces of anything, but the sick woman continued to cry out in pain. They quickly summoned a doctor. After examining her for a while, he said, "It's just delirium, caused by evil entering the pericardium." Her family had long heard of the strangeness of old woman Xu and did not believe the doctor's words. So after the woman died, they went to the Xu family to argue. However, since the matter was bizarre and there was no real evidence, they could not say that the woman was killed by the old woman. After Lu Lian persuaded them, they gave up. However, the fearful hearts of the neighbors were even more intense because of this. They discussed putting the old woman to death. The old woman's son, Sheng Bao, had already expressed his agreement, but her husband insisted on opposing it. The group's discussion was then dropped. Now the old woman is confined in her room by her husband, forbidden to take a single step. And so nothing unusual has happened. But her abnormal words and actions are still the same as before. In the heat of summer, the old woman sleeps soundly wrapped in quilts, unaware of the heat. No one knows what disease she has.

Announcement of Goldfish Exhibition

— Wu Jiren

Suzhou Park, in order to meet the needs of the times and develop public undertakings, holds a recreational gathering once a month. The recreational guidelines are based on openness and interest. Last month, there was a chrysanthemum exhibition, which was one such event. Goldfish are products that cultivate sentiment and temperament and are loved by most people. It is even more indispensable to use them to decorate gardens, ponds, and pools. However, this creature is not easy to raise. Without specialized experience, it is difficult to hope for its long-term survival, which is even more difficult than cultivating flowers and plants. The park originally had more than ten varieties of goldfish, and employed a fish farmer to raise them, which has long been the focus of attention of visitors. Now there is also the creation of this fair, which is also an unprecedented event. It is said that the park is currently entrusting people to widely collect fine varieties from the Shanghai and Huzhou areas, and many goldfish gardens in the Suzhou area are also happy to join.

Recent News from the Silver Screen

After Watching "Robin Hood" A few days ago, I was invited by Mr. Xu of the Carlton to watch the preview of the colorful blockbuster "Robin Hood". Afterwards, Mr. Xu asked me to write an article to praise it. What I want to say is that the brilliance of this film is concentrated in the male lead, Lawrence Tibbett. The greatness of this film is also the greatness of Tibbett himself. Tibbett is not only the pride of the greenwoods, but also the darling of heaven. Tibbett is the most robust and heroic man among men, unparalleled in the world. Tibbett's singing voice, its grandeur and depth, should only be rivaled by the song saint Caruso. As for the magnificence of his physique, it can be seen when he is flogged. He is truly the most beautiful and robust man in the world. Who can compare to him? It is fitting to call him the pride of the greenwoods, and why not the darling of heaven? If anyone still has doubts about this, those doubts can be dispelled after watching Tibbett in this film. Tibbett was originally a famous baritone in the New York Metropolitan Opera Company. This time, he was unexpectedly recruited by Metro Pictures, and he was able to use the introduction of sound film to transfer his divinely bestowed magnificent singing voice to the silver screen. Our desire for auditory and visual pleasure is satisfied, how can we not rejoice? As for the exquisite arrangement of the entire colorful film, etc., these are all minor matters and need not be mentioned. (Jin Xu)

After Watching the Preview of "A Woman of Affairs" The world's morals are declining, and lust is rampant. Observe the young men and women of recent years. Whenever love is mentioned, they are delighted and excited. This is truly regrettable. After I watched the film "A Woman of Affairs," I felt even more deeply about this. The film stars John Gilbert and tells the story of a纨绔子弟 who relies on his wicked money and seductive skills to act capriciously, only knowing how to toy with women. He even thinks of seducing his friend's fiancée. One wrong thought leads to all kinds of tragedies. The discarded old flame commits suicide because of it, and the lover's husband also loses his life because of this. Although he is able to realize his mistakes and repent in the end, the stain on his conscience can never be erased. This is a rough sketch of the film's plot, truly a photographic depiction of a wicked society. John Gilbert has always been known for his skill in playing romantic roles. Anyone who has seen "Flesh and the Devil" and "Love" has a considerable understanding of his artistry. In "A Woman of Affairs," his performance is even more profound, and his demeanor is even more unrestrained than before. His romantic warmth in his dissolute times is intoxicating, and his melancholy and anger during his repentance are also enough to move people deeply. From beginning to end, his performance is impeccable. It is said that the film has already been released to the public at the Paris Grand Theatre. (Ban Yun)

Record of a Strange Snake

— Junshuo

A guest, Gu Mengxian, from Shaoxing, recounted that when he was young, he drank at his relative Yan Qi's home at an elegant gathering to admire orchids. A certain official in the county, recently returned from Shanxi, brought Fenjiu, and ordered his servant to bring it out to entertain his friends. The color was oily and emerald green, called Bamboo Leaf Green. The guests all agreed that using fine wine to appreciate famous flowers made this gathering truly worthwhile. A guest, Mr. Zhang, said, "Bamboo Leaf Green is originally an ancient name, and this wine is very fitting. However, there is also a venomous snake also named Bamboo Leaf Green. I heard from the elders that there was a farmer in my hometown who farmed in the mountain fields, constantly going in and out of the mountains. In the mountains, there was a small snake, no more than two inches long, with a pure green color. Its venom was even more potent than that of a viper. It was said to be a Bamboo Leaf Green. People avoided it. One day, after the rain had cleared, the farmer had something to do in the mountains and wore nailed boots. As he passed through the thick grass, he saw a giant python, more than ten feet long, rolling on the ground, as if in pain. Upon closer inspection, he saw that there was a Bamboo Leaf Green on the head of the giant python. The farmer thought to save the python and quickly lifted his foot to kick it away. The farmer was not unaware of the extreme venom of the Bamboo Leaf Green. He thought that the bottom of his nailed boots had several layers of leather and was lined with iron nails, so there should be no harm. After kicking the Bamboo Leaf Green to the ground, he trampled it to death. The giant python then leisurely departed. When the farmer returned home, his foot was swollen and painful. Before long, the swelling had reached his abdomen. His family asked and learned that it was caused by kicking the Bamboo Leaf Green. They were alarmed and at a loss. As it was getting dark, they suddenly saw a giant python enter through the window, holding several leaves of green grass in its mouth and placing them on the ground. The family was shocked to see the python and turned to flee, but the giant python had already left. The farmer said, 'That was the python from before. It must have brought antidote grass to save me.' He then decocted the grass and drank it. The pain quickly subsided, and he washed his foot with it. By midnight, it had returned to normal, and he was unharmed. Upon examining the shape of the grass, he could not find it again in the mountains. Some say that it probably grows in deep valleys that cannot be reached by human footprints." After Mr. Zhang finished speaking, each of the guests drank a cup and said, "This Bamboo Leaf Green is not like that Bamboo Leaf Green; it can be taken into the stomach." Mengxian said that Mr. Zhang was also from Shaoxing.

Travel Notes from Southeast Asia (83)

— Linghua

On the 31st, I went from the market to the post office. The postal service here falls under the jurisdiction of the Indian government. One shield is equivalent to 1.3 yuan in our currency. I bought stamps for sixteen annas. One anna can send a letter to this port, two annas can send a letter to the British Straits Settlements, and three annas can send a letter to England and Shanghai. There are many women in the market. They wear their hair high and are pleased with their beautiful makeup, comparable to Chinese women. The status of Burmese women is higher than in other places. They are all literate and educated. They guide men. It is said that Burma is the country in the world where people are most afraid of their wives. There are only female staff in the government offices, but their method of applying powder is too crude, to the point of applying it like actors.

I have gained a new observation on the clothing of Burmese men and women, that is, the Burmese have completely become matriarchal and feminized. Burmese men also wear green skirts, with little difference from women, and the same goes for the upper body. They wear all kinds of colorful clothes, so from a distance, there is no difference between men's and women's clothing. What's even stranger is that Burmese men wear flat-topped hats, which look no different from women's high buns. From this, we know that men's clothing, from head to toe, is all learned from their mothers.

There are many Chinese men here who marry Burmese women, and many of the children born abroad have Burmese mothers. However, it is said that Chinese often return home halfway and abandon their wives. Burmese women deeply hate the unconscionability of the Chinese and dare not approach them easily.

On July 1st, Dharma Master Wan invited me to eat at a restaurant. The dishes were very expensive, each dish costing at least one and a half shields, making life more expensive than in Singapore and Penang. In Singapore, I saw 吉能 people (Indian laborers) grabbing rice and vegetables with their hands to eat, which I found very strange. I often ate their pancakes, which were very delicious, at the 吉能 restaurants. They always took the food into their mouths with their hands and washed their hands with water after eating. We found it inconvenient, so they specially provided Western-style knives and forks for the Chinese to use. But in Burma, those restaurants don't often have knives and forks. Everyone grabs the food with their hands, which we find very inconvenient. But those who have been in Southeast Asia for a long time have also adapted to it. Walking on the street, everyone eats outdoors. There was a young Western woman, probably in her twenties, dressed in beautiful clothes, eating oil and meat dishes with her right hand, just like a Burmese woman. I wanted to laugh but didn't dare to. I just recited Ban Gu's "Eastern Capital Rhapsody" and sighed, "How painful it is that customs change people!"

Warmth in My Heart (322)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Sixteen: Cui Xiu Diligently Asks for Characters from the Teacher, Heroic Soldiers Talk Boldly at a Brothel Banquet for Heroines

Let's say that ever since Zuo Shichen met Lvyi at the Yuebin Restaurant, it was as if he had been bewitched again. Adding to this the encouragement from friends, they arranged to eat dinner together every day. You invite me, I invite you, and so on, in a continuous chain. Each time they ate dinner, they felt it was too boring without any women present, so the two had more opportunities to get close. Many organizations in Shanghai are now moving towards Europeanization and do not provide meals and accommodation. People who work in companies and banks during the day often travel a long way home to eat. Some also organize their own places to eat. After five o'clock in the evening, some firms leave one or two employees to watch over, while others simply hand over the door to the "iron general" (lock). They don't care about anything else. After the employees leave, they are finally free to relax. Editors in newspaper offices are exactly the opposite of those people. The time when those people finish work is the time when they start work. Therefore, those editors in newspaper offices, along with the patrolling policemen who keep watch on the streets at night, the female workers who work the night shift in silk factories, and the pig slaughterers in the slaughterhouses, are all nocturnal animals. Sometimes, they work until dawn and go home to eat some porridge and snacks. It's already broad daylight. The next day, they sleep until after lunch. They get up, wash up, eat, and then look at the newspaper they edited to see if there are any problems. After blinking their eyes, the sun sets again. It's time to work again. Dinner time is considered a brief respite where they can relax and enjoy themselves. The first batch of news has already been sent out. The newspapers need to be typeset and won't be on the market until after twelve o'clock. Although the newspaper office also prepares dinner, several senior staff members are unwilling to eat dinner in the newspaper office. There's a reason for this. Because the newspaper office at that time was cramped. The typesetting room and machine room were already very crowded. There was no room for a kitchen. Since there was no kitchen, they had to eat packaged meals. Those packaged meals were really hard to swallow. First of all, just looking at them made one feel that they were unsanitary. In the summer, it's even worse. Flies often looked like black rice and were found in the food. People who suffered from cholera vomiting and diarrhea always suspected that there was something wrong with the packaged meals. In the winter, people always want to eat some warm soup and hot rice. However, after the packaged meals were delivered there, or if there was a delay, the rice and vegetables had already become cold. It felt like a cold-faced, heartless guest had entered one's warm stomach. It was really difficult to digest. Secondly, the dishes cooked by the packaged meal service were cooked in a large pot. The bigger the packaged meal service, the more meals they provided, and the dishes were all the same. One table had these few dishes, and another table had the same few dishes. They fed thousands of people every day. Therefore, the fish and meat all tasted the same. Moreover, the rice was also of inferior quality and was not cooked to the right consistency. Therefore, even when the waiter came to invite them to eat dinner, they could only leave with a sigh.

Commercial News

Gold Price Soars by Ten Taels

Rapid Rise, Optimistic Outlook

The Situation Develops Greatly Yesterday, the 25th, the bidding price of gold rose sharply, exceeding 590 taels, a significant increase of more than ten taels. The rise was orderly and steady. In the morning session, there was a difference of about six taels. In the afternoon session, there was a swing of only two taels. The situation developed greatly. The exchange rate was somewhat weak, with the listed price shrinking by one level in both the morning and afternoon sessions. The industry was struggling, and the market was seeking to replenish supplies. Yuan Maoyong, Yuan Chengyong, and others were all competing to buy, while sellers included Zhifeng, Yongwanxing, and Yuanli. Overseas silver prices were low, indicating that the gold price would open high. Afterwards, there was only a fluctuation of one tael, and the rise was rapid, soaring straight up. By noon, it had risen by five taels, reaching above ninety-six taels. In the afternoon session, Dadecheng, Tong Taichang, and others were buying, while Heng Fuchang, Xie Yu, and others were selling. The exchange rate was particularly weak and tight, both officially and unofficially. The industry continued to struggle. However, the gold price fluctuated from time to time, probably due to the different buying and selling. In the end, it was extremely sharp, exceeding ninety-eight taels. Since the swap, it has been at a new high price, and the future is still optimistic. It is said that the bulk orders this morning will definitely be lower.

The Market Climbs Steadily The opening price of gold for the month of January this morning was 590 taels and nine qian, already up two taels and eight qian. The gross price was ninety to ninety-one taels, and then it retreated by one tael. Yuan Maoyong, Yuan Chengyong, and others were buying, while Shunli, Wanxing, Taikangrun, and others were selling. The price of bulk orders and silver had fallen by one-eighth. Afterwards, buyers were not idle, and it rose to ninety-one taels and six qian. Shile Island, which has been out of stock for a long time, sold out yesterday at an opening price of 3 qian 6 fen and a half. Among the colored strips, Fei Lian and two colors are the most popular. Hanshan Temple Seven Treasure Beads bald color already requires 7 taels and 2 qian. The bald blue stripe is still at 6 taels and 6 qian and a half. The decline in blue stripe cashmere is very fierce, with Ersunfu falling to 5 taels and 1 qian, and Denggao at 5 taels and 1 qian and a half. Local News

Continued Record of Internal Debt Creditor Group News

Expected to be Formally Established Within the Month

Preliminary Procedures are Underway for Registration

The Shanghai Banking Association initiated the organization of the Internal Debt Creditor Group, which was detailed in yesterday's newspaper. Yesterday, this newspaper's reporter specially visited Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Commerce and Industry and Standing Committee Member of the Banking Association, to inquire about everything in detail. According to his reply, the main purpose of the Banking Association's initiation of the Internal Debt Creditor Group is to ensure that internal and external debts enjoy absolutely equal rights. According to government statistics, the total amount of internal and external debts is approximately 1.3 billion yuan, with internal debt accounting for slightly more than 30% of the total and external debt accounting for slightly less than 70%. However, the Nishihara loans of more than 200 million yuan are not included. The Internal Debt Creditor Group will be formally established after the representatives of the banks in Beiping and Tianjin arrive. It is expected to be completed within the month. After the establishment of the creditor group, the first step will be to conduct a joint registration of national internal debt creditors. All non-banking creditors can come to register. Then, a general meeting will be convened to elect formal representatives to discuss reorganization measures with the Ministry of Finance. The statement that the Internal and External Debt Reorganization Committee will hold a meeting in Shanghai and that banking representatives will attend is completely inaccurate, he said.

Internal and External Debt Reorganization Meeting

No Meeting Held Yesterday

Li Sihao Has Not Yet Taken Office

There were rumors that the Internal and External Debt Reorganization Committee continued to hold a reorganization meeting in Shanghai yesterday. Yesterday, this newspaper's reporter specially interviewed a certain important figure in the Ministry of Finance. According to him, there was no meeting of any kind today (the 25th). Minister Song was originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai from Nanjing at 3:00 p.m., but he did not come temporarily. Therefore, it was impossible to attend the meeting. As for when and where the newly appointed Chairman of the Internal and External Debt Reorganization Committee, Mr. Li Sihao, will take office, there is currently no news, he said. The various important pieces of news are compiled and recorded as follows:

Xin Sheng She (New Voice Society) said that the Ministry of Finance has made detailed plans for reorganizing internal and external debts and has drafted a plan to announce to internal and external debt creditors. It is heard that the methods and time limits for the order of repayment of various debts, whether secured or unsecured, have been determined. The repayment period for both internal and external debts is set at 30 years. Regarding the internal debt portion, it is limited to those issued by the government through the Ministry of Finance. Other debts, such as the former Ministry of Transportation's Transportation Public Bonds, Electrical Public Bonds, and provincial bonds, are not within the scope of this reorganization.

Ri Ri She (Daily News) said that national unification and the pacification of wars make the reorganization of internal and external debts an essential plan for financial management. The reorganization of external debts was held in Nanjing on the 15th. The principles put forward by our side are nothing more than slightly flattening the interest rates of the various debts, earlier and later, and designating one of the national tax revenue items specified by the central government as a source of funds for installment payments. The predetermined time limit should not exceed 30 years at the latest. As a result of the meeting of Chinese and foreign representatives, it was decided that each country would proceed separately and independently. If necessary, meetings would be convened to resolve the issues. It is understood that the reason for this is Japan's Nishihara loans. These loans were provided during the Beiping government era by Japan to promote internal strife in China. They have no legal basis, and the National Government has long declared their repudiation and has issued a memorandum to the Japanese government. However, the Japanese side still included the Nishihara loans this time, so it should negotiate with the Japanese side separately to abolish them. In addition, as for the Hukuang loans, they were divided among the four countries of England, France, the United States, and Germany in 1911. Now, the majority of the debts have been merged into the United States. Therefore, the US side pays special attention to the principles put forward to our country. According to information from a certain party, our country's foreign debts have increased due to the soaring gold prices. It is heard that our country plans to implement the collection of gold for imports after the new customs tariff is promulgated as a way to offset foreign debts so as not to suffer losses.

Shanghai-Yichang Aviation

Officially Flies on December 16th

China National Aviation Corporation has now decided to expand the Shanghai-Hankou air route to Yichang and has scheduled to officially fly beginning on the 16th of next month. China National Aviation Corporation originally planned to expand the Shanghai-Hankou line to Chongqing in October. However, due to Liu Xiang's opposition, the Ministry of Transportation sent Nie Kaiyi, Deputy Director of the Airline Group of the Airline Corporation, to Sichuan to discuss the matter with Liu Xiang. Liu Xiang expressed to Nie that he did not object to Shanghai-Chongqing aviation. However, the use of personnel and administration at the Chongqing air station must be controlled by the Sichuan side, and even the planes must be commanded by Liu. In that case, if necessary, Shanghai-Chongqing planes could be seized in Chongqing for military use. Mr. Nie returned because the negotiations were unsuccessful. The Shanghai-Chongqing aviation business was also temporarily suspended. Now, in order to develop the aviation business, China National Aviation Corporation has decided to first operate the Shanghai-Yichang route. The flight details have also been specified, which will divide the Shanghai-Yichang line into two sections. The Shanghai-Hankou section will remain the same, with daily round-trip flights except on Sundays. The Hankou-Yichang section is now scheduled to fly round-trip once every Monday, Wednesday, Friday, Saturday, and Thursday. The plane will take off from Hankou at 8:15 a.m. and arrive in Yichang at 10:30 a.m. The plane will fly from Yichang at 11:00 a.m. and arrive in Hankou at 1:15 p.m. The one-way fare is 52 yuan per passenger, and the round-trip fare is 78 yuan.

Shanghai-Wenzhou Restores Freight Transportation Starting Today

The Wenzhou Strike Ban Wave is Resolved

Foreign and Guangdong Goods are Still Not Subject to Unified Tax

The Yongjia Unified Donation Bureau merged the Wenzhou Foreign and Guangdong Goods Donation and changed it to a Unified Tax, which triggered a strike and transportation wave. It has been nine days since the 17th. No Wenzhou goods have been transported, ships have been emptied, workers have been laid off, and the obstruction of goods has affected the market, which is not insignificant. Yesterday afternoon, Shanghai received a telegram from Wenzhou stating that the rejection donation and strike transportation wave had ended. The information obtained from various parties after investigation is recorded as follows:

Tax Bureau Stops Collecting Unified Donations The outbreak of this wave was due to the change of Foreign and Guangdong Goods Donations to Unified Tax. According to the old rules, for every 100 yuan of goods, donations and taxes must be increased, ranging from 6 yuan and 6 jiao to 10 yuan. Each commercial firm refused to acknowledge it because it was too heavy a burden. Therefore, it used strike transportation and suspension of business as a means to demand the cessation of changes. The tax bureau initially refused to cancel it and confronted the commercial groups. Neither side would budge. After ten days (since the merger on the 16th), it was heard that each store would further cease operations. It was not until yesterday that the Chamber of Commerce came forward to mediate. Foreign and Guangdong goods will still be taxed according to the original tax rules, and the change to a Unified Tax will be abolished. The tax bureau expressed its agreement, and the Chamber of Commerce immediately notified each commercial firm to cancel the strike transportation.

Commercial Groups Cancel Strike Transportation Yesterday afternoon, the Wenzhou group received a telegram from Oujiang stating that the foreign and Guangdong taxes were still levied according to the old rules and that the purpose of the request had been achieved. The various industries' strike transportation and boycott will stop on the 25th. Beginning today, all Wenzhou export goods will be declared, loaded, and taxed as usual. The dock workers will also resume work starting today. The goods to be shipped from Shanghai can be transported as much as possible. A major wave has come to an end.

Accumulated Goods Rushed to Load and Transport to Shanghai The China Merchants Bureau Haiyan and Guangji ships have been emptied three times, losing at least seven or eight thousand yuan. Yesterday afternoon, they received a telegram from Wenzhou stating that the tax matter had been resolved and that the goods accumulated in Wenzhou were plentiful. Starting on the 26th, loading can begin. Shanghai has also notified each customer to quickly declare and transport the goods that have been detained. A large wave has come to an end.

Italian Industrial Tourism Group to Arrive in Shanghai

Expected to Arrive on the 7th of Next Month

Since this year, Italy has been actively promoting Sino-Italian commerce, starting with expanding its shipping industry as a pioneer for developing its commercial and trade promotion in East Asia. Now, it has also organized a tourism group to come to China for inspection. What we have heard is recorded below:

Expanding the Shipping Industry: On the route between China and Italy, only one shipping company used to operate, dispatching six ships for voyages. Last year, four newly built motor vessels were added to sail to Shanghai. This autumn, the Italian Lloyd Triestino Shipping Company, with subsidies from the Italian government, began expanding its shipping business in the Far East. Recognizing the global trend of fast ships, it specifically divided the China-Italy route into two classes: mail ships and cargo ships. It removed the ships with smaller horsepower and replaced them with five purely passenger ships with high speed: the "Conte Verde," "Piero Toselli," "Conte Rosso," "Conte Biancamano," and "Viminale," to operate the mail ship service. This reduces the sea journey between China and Italy from the previous 38 or 39 days to 28 days. Another four ships will be dispatched to specialize in cargo for the Far East. The new ships are about to arrive. Sino-Italian merchant ships have thus leaped to become Royal Mail Ships.

Organizing a Tourism Group: With the expansion of shipping having been realized, the country is also starting to seek progress in trade with China. A Far East Tourism Group was organized by leaders of domestic manufacturers, factories, and import-export businesses. Its purpose is to promote Italian goods to the Far East, specifically coming to Shanghai and other places for inspection. The group has a total of 300 members and has already departed from Italy, having taken the Italian mail ship "Conte Verde" to Shanghai. Yesterday, this local newspaper received news that it has passed Singapore and will arrive in Shanghai at 9:00 AM on December 7th. The group members are mostly from the Italian industrial sector, but people from other Western countries have also joined. After inspecting Shanghai, they will go to the capital and then to Japan, it is said.

Shanghai Circles Oppose Opium Poppy Planting in Fujian

Holding a Joint Meeting

Advocating Thorough Resistance

The Chinese National Anti-Drug Association states that the Fujian garrison is encouraging the planting of opium poppies in order to collect opium seedling taxes. The public groups in Fujian resisted this, but to no avail. The local garrison is still actively collecting taxes. At the request of various groups in Fujian, a joint meeting of all circles was held yesterday at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. The mood was exceptionally indignant, and many proposals were made by various groups. The situation of the conference is recorded below:

Participating Groups: Fujian Fellow Villagers Association in Beijing, Fujian Fellow Villagers Association in Shanghai, Fujian Academic Association in Shanghai, United Association of All Circles in Xiamen, Chinese Overseas Affairs Advancement Association, Shanghai Jin-Hui Guildhall, Road Construction Association, Quanzhou Fellow Villagers Association in Zhejiang, Fujian Journalists Association, Lijiiao Joint Association, Shanghai Young Women's Christian Association, Youth Preaching Group, Chinese Red Cross Society, Chinese Medical Association, Universal Student Association, and 36 other groups, with over 60 representatives.

Representatives' Reports: The meeting started as scheduled at 4:00 PM. Huang Jiahuai, the general secretary of the Chinese National Anti-Drug Association, and Zhou Chucai, the director of the investigation department, successively reported on the recent situation of opium poppy planting in southern Fujian. In summary, they stated that the situation of opium poppy planting in southern Fujian has been reported by the public, and by major newspapers, and by the investigations of the Anti-Drug Association. The counties of Putian, Xianyou, and Hui'an, the districts of Zhangzhou, the villages of Fuding, and the area of Jinjiang have all been planted with opium poppies. The Zhang-Tong-Yan Pacification Office has been established to collect opium taxes, and the situation is urgent. Therefore, all representatives attending the meeting today should urgently discuss response methods. Subsequently, representatives from the Fujian Fellow Villagers Association in Beijing, the Fujian Anti-Drug Branch Association, the Fujian Journalists Association, the Penang Save Fujian United Association, the Fujian Academic Association in Shanghai, the Fujian Fellow Villagers Association in Shanghai, and the United Association of All Circles in Xiamen reported successively. Generally, they said that the planting of opium poppies is prevalent in Jinjiang County, Fujian, with the thirteen villages of Maping being the main source of the disaster. In Hui'an County, the opium seedlings are two or three inches tall from Fengting to Huicheng. In Tong'an County, opium poppies have been planted in more than forty villages, including the Lubanwei area of the Xinxu Public Security District. Opium seedlings have also been found in various villages in Nan'an County. In other areas, such as Xiangtian Lotus Mountain in Xianyou County, Meizhou in Zhao'an County, Dongsha Township in Tian County, and Yangzhongchen and Shangxia Kan villages in Ningde County, opium seedlings have also been discovered. The Fujian Provincial Government sacrificed four million opium seedling tax revenue to strictly prohibit opium poppy planting in the past, and only now has there been a glimmer of hope. Now, the counties in southern Fujian are still covered with opium seedlings. If the news spreads and other areas follow suit, the situation will spread like wildfire, poisoning the entire province and causing endless harm. Moreover, the garrison detachments are collecting opium taxes, totaling one million yuan in Zhangzhou and Tong'an, and hundreds of thousands of yuan in Jinjiang and Xianyou. The remote areas are not even worth mentioning. Even on both sides of the Quanan Zhangma highway, which passes through bustling and convenient transportation routes, opium seedlings have been found. The Fujian Anti-Opium Committee is perfunctory, and should be reorganized as soon as possible.

Important Resolutions: The attending representatives proposed many motions. The resolutions that were passed are recorded below: (1) The representative of the Fuzhou Journalists Association proposed: (A) Request the government to reorganize the Fujian Anti-Opium Committee; (B) Strictly organize the Fujian Anti-Drug Branch Association; (C) Request the Fujian Provincial Government to issue a general order to all counties to establish opium detoxification hospitals to accommodate opium addicts; (D) Request the Fujian Provincial Government to severely punish the Japanese opium dens in Fuzhou that condone opium use. Resolution: Passed. (2) The Quanzhou Fellow Villagers Association in Zhejiang proposed: Request the central government to transfer the garrison that is forcing opium poppy planting and collecting taxes, and temporarily dispatch a disciplined and trained army to Fujian to take full responsibility for opium prohibition until the opium seedlings are eradicated. Resolution: Passed. (3) The overseas Chinese groups in Penang and the Save Fujian United Association proposed: Request the central government to send personnel to thoroughly investigate the military personnel in the opium seedling areas to rectify discipline. Resolution: Passed. (4) The United Association of All Circles in Xiamen and the Fujian Academic Association in Shanghai proposed: Request the government to strictly arrest Zhang Yongshun, a local opium trafficker in Xiamen, and severely punish him according to the law, and report to the League of Nations. Resolution: Passed. (5) The Shanghai Medical Association proposed: Investigate the evidence of Zhang Yongshun's drug trafficking, revoke his medical qualification, and request the Ministry of Health to pay attention to the amount of drugs purchased by doctors. Resolution: Passed. For the above cases, the Shanghai Fellow Villagers Association, the Beijing Fellow Villagers Association in Shanghai, and the Fujian Academic Association in Shanghai were publicly elected to form another committee to be responsible for implementation.
