Ministry's Approval of Half-Price Coal Freight

Restoring Original Price from the First of This Month

The China National Coal Production and Sales Association received a directive No. 591 from the Ministry of Railways yesterday, stating: Having received the report and investigated, the Jiaoji Railway Management Committee previously temporarily suspended the export freight rate of coal on the line upon approval from the Ministry, because the coal shortage in Shandong Province was in urgent need of relief, and unscrupulous merchants were still taking advantage of the low export freight rate to transport stored coal out of the province regardless of the overall situation, so that foreign coal could take the opportunity to enter and flood various markets in Shandong Province. This measure was purely for relieving the coal shortage in Shandong Province and preventing foreign coal from seizing the market for domestic coal, and was of a temporary nature, not intended to increase railway revenue. It has now been reported by the committee that the supply and demand of coal in various parts of Shandong Province has been corresponding in recent months, and the export freight rate of coal on the line was restored on November 1st. The directive from the Ministry approved this to be filed for record. Now, according to the report stating the previous situation, this directive is hereby issued for notification.

Proposed by Chairman Chiang

Passed by the Assembly

The Name of the Shanghai Municipal Council Education Department to Be Changed Soon

Explanation by Liu Zhan'en and Others

Local people have declared their opposition to this matter, and it has been reported in the newspapers repeatedly. On the 13th of this month, the Executive Committee of the Third District of the Kuomintang even published an advertisement questioning Zhan'en and others. There may be some misunderstandings in the questions. The process is briefly described below. After Shanghai Public Concession Shanghai Ratepayers' Association, on March 26, 1928, contained a clause that "Under the current situation, the responsibility of expanding the education of Chinese people in the concession should be emphasized," the settlement organized a design agency called the Education Committee this year. The English name is "Board of Education." There are three Chinese members, four Western members, and one Japanese member. There are also Chinese directors and Chinese committee members, and Zhan'en and others were recommended to participate in the committee. Zhan'en and others believed that under the current situation in the settlement, there were too many people who did not attend school. It is necessary to urgently promote education so that the education of Chinese people in the settlement and national education can gradually converge. However, in order to promote education, it is necessary to first clarify the current situation of education in the settlement, otherwise there is no basis. This is the origin of the publication of the survey. As for the Shanghai Municipal Council issuing a letter of investigation in the name of the Education Department, it was not a resolution of the Education Committee, and Zhan'en and others had never heard of it. Because the Shanghai Municipal Council originally had an Education Department, those who translated Chinese used the word "Department" for the police, health, and other agencies of the Shanghai Municipal Council. Therefore, it was translated as "Department." After this matter was discovered, Zhan'en and others thought it was inappropriate and immediately proposed a change. It should be changed soon. We are grateful for the guidance from all walks of life, which shows the utmost concern for the education of Chinese people in the settlement and the importance of correcting names. We hereby announce the facts in accordance with the truth, and we hope that you will understand and observe.

Sino-Foreign Joint Ventures May Appoint Representatives to Join the Chamber of Commerce

But Must Be Subject to Four Restrictions

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday notified the various trade associations: We hereby inform you that on the 24th of this month, we received Instruction No. 13955 from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, stating: In the case of the Qingdao Telegram, the Committee for the Reorganization of Iron and Steel Machinery Industry Groups inquired whether the Chinese managers of foreign-owned machinery factories and the Chinese managers of Sino-foreign joint ventures can join the Chamber of Commerce as members, and requested compliance. It was considered that whether it could be allowed had not been expressly stipulated, so opinions were prepared and submitted, allowing them to appoint representatives to join the Chamber of Commerce, but subject to three restrictions, and submitted to the Executive Yuan. Order No. 11442 from the Training Department of the Central Executive Committee stated: After reviewing the three measures drafted by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, Item 1, the representative appointed should be limited to citizens of the Republic of China according to law, and Item 2, more than half of the capital of the company or store must be Chinese shares, there is nothing inappropriate, and three more items should be added, namely, the Chinese side of the company or store must have more than half of the voting rights, and Item 3 of the original draft, more than half of the directors of the company must be citizens of the Republic of China, should be changed to Item 4, and ordered to comply, etc. Having received this order, in addition to submitting a reply, we hereby order your association to notify and comply. The city's Sino-foreign joint venture stores are probably not limited to the iron and steel machinery industry alone. Therefore, according to the previous cause, if such stores in various industries request to join the trade association in the future, they can be handled accordingly. In addition to sending separate letters, we hereby send this letter for your information and compliance.

US Raw Silk Import Report

The Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau Raw Silk Inspection Office of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce received a report from the Silk Association of America yesterday, stating that the total import of raw silk in the United States from June 1 last year to the end of June this year was 568,038 dan, including 465,649 dan of Japanese silk, a decrease of 11.05% compared to the previous year; 48,803 dan of Shanghai factory silk and gray silk, an increase of 62.08% compared to the previous year; 34,322 dan of Guangdong silk, an increase of 23.07% compared to the previous year; and 19,264 dan of European silk, an increase of 16.07% compared to the previous year.

Baoshan County Administration Meeting

Baoshan County Magistrate Qiu Mingjiu convened a county administration meeting at the county government yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM, inviting the heads of the subordinate bureaus and sections. The attendees included Xu Xiangye of the Public Security Bureau, Bei Jitai, head of the Finance Bureau, Pu Wengui, head of the Education Bureau, Tian, head of the Construction Bureau, Wang Tongchuan, head of the first section of the county government, Xue Ying, head of the second section, Ji Zhonghe, director of the agricultural field, Yin Shuqi, head of the roster bureau, Chairman County Magistrate Qiu, and recorder Zhang Ruyu. Matters for discussion, one item, directive No. 1933.1041 from the Construction and Finance Bureaus, ordering the county to raise the first phase of construction public bonds. The provincial government meeting decided that the county would be allocated 50,000 yuan, and stipulated that the end of November would be the first phase, the end of December would be the second phase, and the end of January would be the third phase. One third of each phase must be turned in. The deadline is near and imminent. How should this be handled? Please decide. (Resolution) It should be borne by the county's agricultural and commercial sectors, with agriculture accounting for 70% and commerce accounting for 30%. The 70% of the agricultural burden should be allocated according to the number of acres. Farmers with less than five acres of farmland will be exempt from the allocation. Detailed measures will be decided after convening a meeting of the district heads. One item, the public schools of the county government and various bureaus will end at the end of the month. Please issue student awards. (Resolution) The county government will subsidize 5 yuan for award fees, and each bureau will subsidize 2.5 yuan, totaling 15 yuan, to be handled by the presiding staff.

Large Number of Returning Japanese Marines

Four hundred marine soldiers specially dispatched by the Japanese government to Shanghai, stationed in the Hongkou area to protect Japanese expatriates for several years, are now being fully transferred back to the original defense of Sasebo by the Army Ministry with the approval of Colonel Shibayama, commander of the Marines. This is because the situation is now peaceful and the Japanese are living and working in peace, and there is no need to send heavy troops. Yesterday, they left Shanghai on the Nojima special service ship. Many Japanese expatriates and gentry went to the Huishan Wharf to see them off. At present, only a portion of the soldiers from the warships remain in Shanghai.

Recent News on the Reorganization of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company

Goods from Henan Can Now Be Shipped to Shanghai

Li Zhonggong, the new general manager of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, has begun to reorganize the business. In recent days, he has begun to change branch managers, business directors, etc., in order to help implement the resumption of shifts and revitalize the bureau affairs on the first of next month. The information obtained is recorded below:

Removal of Bureau Chiefs: After the removal of Wang Hao, director of the Hankou Bureau, and the reassignment of Li Yunliang, an order was issued yesterday to the secretarial and affairs departments to review the handover report of Wang Quan. At present, the bureau chiefs along the Yangtze River are being reorganized first, and those who are not working effectively will be changed. Chongqing is an important port in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, and a capable person must be in charge to compete with foreign ships. The original director, Zhu Biqian, has been removed and Liu Weizhao has been appointed to replace him. In addition, Feng Jingwu, the director of the Zhenjiang Bureau, has resigned and Guo Yanmo has been appointed to succeed him. He went to Zhenjiang yesterday to take over. Several more branch offices will be removed and transferred in the coming days.

Change of Captains: Captain He Hailan, a fair ship captain, was ordered by Li Zhonggong to transfer to the ship affairs section, and Jin Yueshi was appointed to replace him. Captain Chen Fayu of the Jiangtian ship will be assigned to another position, and Qin Fanshi will be appointed to replace him. Zhang Zhongyu, the business director of the Jiangda ship, will be replaced by Gu Tingyuan. Yesterday, the resignation of Xu Yankang, the business director of the Xinjiangtian ship, was approved and Zhang Yuqian was appointed to replace him. The handover has been completed. It is also heard that General Manager Li proposed at the last bureau affairs meeting that many business directors must be replaced. He must wait for his return to Shanghai from Beijing before announcing the changes one after another.

Business on the Yangtze River: Business on the Yangtze River is the lifeblood of the bureau. All the ships on the Yangtze River will be fully restored, and the branch directors in each port will be ordered to actively transport cargo in order to save the lost shipping rights. According to a telegram from Director Li of the Hankou Bureau yesterday, the Henan passenger traffic has been opened to transport tobacco from Xuchang, and the right to carry it has been obtained. The first batch of tobacco shipped to Shanghai after the war has more than 10,000 pieces. It was detained by the tax bureau when it was transported to Hankou. It has now been explained by the Hankou Bureau and is expected to be released and loaded onto ships to Shanghai for transshipment to foreign countries.

Jiangsu Construction Department Urges Conscription and Road Construction

The Shanghai County Construction Bureau received a telegram from the Jiangsu Construction Department yesterday, stating that the conscription and road construction and bridge and culvert construction projects are all the responsibility of the bureau. If there are any problems in planning, budgeting, and implementation that are not easy to solve, inquiries should be made by telegram or in person to the province. Except for those that have already started, the bureau is given until the end of this month to prepare all procedures and until December 1 to start construction. There must be no further delays, otherwise the investigation will be carried out. This conscription and road construction will be based on the merit of the achievements. The standards of merit will be determined. Everyone should abide by this and not ignore it.

Negotiation Regarding Shandong Steamer Cutting Off Fishing Boat

Boatmen Consider First Steps for Action

Liu Jinye, a sand fishing boat owner in this port, suffered a significant loss when his boat was cut in half by the British Taikoo Company's Shandong steamer opposite the Yangshupu Flour Mill at 10:30 AM on the 18th of this month. The Shandong steamer reported that the fishing boat had collided with the steamer first, attempting to evade responsibility. It is said that the boatmen are poor and displaced and are planning the first steps for action.

Penalties for Shops in the French Concession Not Affixing Revenue Stamps

Since the establishment of the Stamp Tax Bureau in the French Concession by Commissioners Liu Chunpu and Shen Rulin, they have planned and actively implemented the tax, and the tax revenue has been steadily improving. Merchants and residents in the concession also consider paying taxes a civic duty and are happy to affix stamps to documents such as pawn tickets for pawnshops and rent receipts for rented houses, which are being promoted gradually. If any shops, tempted by petty profits, are found to have omitted stamps on invoices or deliberately failed to issue invoices, the case will be immediately reported to the Stamp Tax Office in Shanghai, which will send a letter to the French Municipal Police to prosecute in the French Court. Previously, four shops, including Yanchang Coal Company, were summoned to court by the police and penalized for not affixing stamps. Commissioners Liu and Shen have now discovered that Hongfa Sugar Company on Yangxing Street issued an invoice for over 1,000 taels without affixing stamps, and that the delivery book of Lao Yida Dyehouse on Avenue Edward VII also failed to affix stamps as required. They reported this to the French Municipal Police, who summoned the parties to court yesterday. Commissioner Liu Chunpu also appeared in court to testify and present the case. Presiding Judge Zhu sentenced Hongfa Sugar Company to a fine of 20 yuan and Lao Yida Dyehouse to a fine of 15 yuan as a warning. Any omissions discovered in the future will be severely penalized.

Petition for Interdiction Case

Yesterday, Cai Changming, accompanied by Cai Shengnan, hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit in the French Court, stating that Cai Changming, the first petitioner, is the younger brother of Cai Changgen, and Cai Shengnan, the second petitioner, is the nephew of Cai Changgen. Recently, Cai Changgen has been ill for a long time and has lost consciousness. His wife, Chen, is about to sell all his property and return to her hometown with the money. Therefore, their lawyer published a notice opposing this. Chen has also hired a lawyer to defend her position. Hence, this urgent petition for interdiction, requesting that the petitioners be appointed as guardians to manage the property, so that it can be returned to Changgen when he recovers. Chen, represented by her lawyer, argued that the statements made by the plaintiff's lawyer are utterly absurd. Cai Changgen's property is actually the property of his wife, Chen. Changgen is ill, but Chen is healthy and naturally has the right to manage the property. According to the law, an interdiction can only be initiated at the request of the person themselves or their spouse. How can a third party come forward to petition for interdiction? It is clearly an attempt to embezzle the property. If they want to seize the property, they should just say so. This kind of request will only be ridiculed by legal professionals across the country. She requested that the petition be rejected. Judge Gong ordered the parties to leave and await a decision. Before the case is concluded, Chen is not allowed to transfer the property without authorization.

Xue's Concubine's Request for Division of Inheritance Still in Mediation

Xue Gu Qiaolin, the concubine of the late famous dye merchant Xue Baorun, and her daughter Xue Baobao, filed a lawsuit through lawyer Zheng Yuxiu, demanding a share of the inheritance that was controlled by the main wife Xue Sun and her son Gansheng, to support their livelihood. This has been reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that lawyer Chen Zemin and Xu Yabo, a relative of Xue Gu Qiaolin, negotiated a mediation yesterday. Chen stated that Xue's estate was not as much as the 1.8 million claimed by the plaintiff, and that it should be calculated based on the remaining assets after deducting debts, which would make an agreement more likely. Xu believed that starting from this point would result in too large of a discrepancy, and suggested that Chen further consult with a prominent figure or Zheng Yuxiu directly, hoping to reach a peaceful settlement before the court hearing, to avoid hurting feelings.

Local News Two

Rally to Support Xiao and Oppose the Dutch

Meeting Today

Time... This afternoon at 1:00 PM

Location... Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Tianhou Palace

Twenty organizations, including the Overseas Chinese Federation and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Advancement Association, jointly initiated the "Rally to Support Xiao and Oppose the Dutch," scheduled to be held at 1:00 PM this afternoon at the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Tianhou Palace Bridge, North Henan Road, Public Concession. Minister Yang of the Municipal Party Department Propaganda Department and others will attend. All newspapers and news agencies, recognizing that this concerns the patriotic movement, will gather to report and take photos. The Foreign Affairs Support Association for Overseas Chinese Expelled from British and Dutch Territories in Nanjing telegraphed that the Overseas Chinese Federation decided to send all members from Beijing to Shanghai to attend. A two-zhang white cloth banner was hung at the gate of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, reading "Shanghai All Circles Support Xiao and Oppose the Dutch Rally." The venue was filled with slogans such as "Down with Dutch Imperialism" and "Boycott Java Steamships," creating a somber atmosphere. The telegrams from Nanjing and Xiamen and the meeting agenda and slogans are transcribed below.

Telegram from Nanjing: Overseas Chinese Federation Anti-Dutch Rally, all members of our association will attend. Special notice, Foreign Affairs Support Association for Overseas Chinese Expelled from British and Dutch Territories, respectfully.

Telegram from Xiamen: Overseas Chinese Federation and all institutions, associations, newspapers, and overseas Chinese, be aware that Dutch imperialists have established companies, sailing into our inland, seizing our profits, invading our shipping, and have long been hated by our people. Recently, they have disbanded our country's Dutch-affiliated party headquarters, expelled our party members, increased entry taxes for Chinese people, restricted Chinese ships from traveling in Dutch territories, banned Chinese party ideology books, and explicitly stipulated that Chinese people are on equal footing with indigenous people in taxation, all kinds of acts of tyranny and intentional insults, which have made our overseas Chinese gnash their teeth. This time, the imperialists have intensified their actions, allowing the first and second officers of their Zhibade ship to forcibly rape Ms. Xiao Xin'an of our country. This kind of animalistic behavior not only destroys women, but also clearly insults our national prestige, which has aroused public outrage across the country. They have risen up to resist. Our association believes that this matter concerns the national prestige. If we do not seize this case and strive to fight for it, what will become of our country's international future? Therefore, on the fish day, we presented it to the Siming County Party Affairs Guidance Committee, dispatching personnel to guide the meeting and discussion, and resolved to organize this association to provide support. Nanyang Commercial Association, Seamen's Branch, Wharf Workers' Union, and Tongren Association, Luo Hai Clearing Workers' Union, Gonghe Club Inn Workers' Union, Sugar and Oil Association, and Minzhan Association and other nine groups were elected as committee members and began work immediately. From Yang Day onwards, all cargo and passengers were stopped for Dutch ships until the goal of punishing the murderers and avenging the shame was achieved. However, fearing that the power of our association is limited and the countermeasures may not be comprehensive, we hope that all circles across the country will unanimously advocate, organize groups, and send urgent telegrams to the government, instructing the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to strictly negotiate in the spirit of revolution to achieve victory. The urgency of this telegram is indescribable. Xiamen Support Xiao Case Committee, respectfully.

Meeting Agenda: (1) Ring the bell to start the meeting. (2) Bow three times to the Party and National Flag and the portrait of the Prime Minister. (3) Elect a temporary presidium. (4) The chairman of the presidium respectfully reads the Prime Minister's will. (5) Silent for three minutes (to commemorate the Prime Minister and mourn tens of thousands of overseas Chinese killed by Dutch soldiers over the years). (6) The chairman announces the purpose of the meeting. (7) The organizer reports on the preparation process. (8) Speeches. (9) Discuss proposals. (10) Pass a constitution and telegrams. (11) Elect representatives to petition in Beijing. (12) Shout slogans. (13) Ring the bell to end the meeting.

Meeting Slogans: (1) Down with Dutch imperialism. (2) Abolish the Sino-Dutch consular treaty. (3) Relieve the suffering of overseas Chinese in Dutch territories. (4) Abolish Article 109 of the Dutch regulations. (5) Boycott Java steamships. (6) Avenge the overseas Chinese who were killed and raped. (7) Severely punish the Dutch rapist gang. (8) The Dutch government should compensate and apologize to our government. (9) Long live the Chinese Kuomintang. (10) Long live the Republic of China.

Emergency Meeting on the Xin Case

Expand Organization and Increase Committee Members

Send Letter to Du Yuesheng Requesting Justice

The Xin Dingxiang Tragedy Support Association held an emergency meeting yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM at the Ningbo Sojourners Association. Representatives from the Citizens' Federation, Postal Workers' Union, Inland Shipping Workers' Union, Newspaper Delivery Workers' Union, Chinese and Foreign Cloth Industry Workers' Union, South Shanghai Cleaning Workers' Union, Chinese Electric Workers' Union, British and American Tobacco Workers' Union, Business Workers' Union, Sixth District Party Department, French Concession Water and Electricity Workers' Union, and Chinese Seamen's Union, as well as Xin Dingxiang's father Xin Hesheng and wife Xin Zhou, totaling over 100 people, attended. Liu Xinquan was elected chairman and Cheng Zhiliang as the recorder. First, the chairman reported on the purpose of convening the emergency meeting. Then, Cheng Zhiliang reported on the details of the Xin case and the recent situation in detail. Xin's wife, Zhou, then stood up and said briefly that since her husband's tragic death, she had been in unbearable pain. Foreigners had cruelly killed her husband, leaving her helpless. She is currently pregnant and will be giving birth soon. Although she does not know whether it will be a boy or a girl, she does not know how she, a widow, will raise the child. The future is bleak. Therefore, since others killed her husband, she must achieve the goal of punishing the murderer in order to let her late husband rest in peace. Secondly, her livelihood has been left unresolved, and she hopes that everyone will uphold justice and actively help, as she feels a life and death connection with everyone. It was then decided that: (1) Secret. (2) Xin Dingxiang's father, Xin Hesheng, must not negotiate with the other party alone, and everything must be resolved by the Support Association. (3) Expand the Support Association's organization: A. Increase the committee to 21 organizations, B. Print and distribute leaflets, C. Establish a speaking team. (4) Decide to add the following thirteen organizations to the Support Association committee: Citizens' Federation, Pharmacy Industry Workers' Union, Postal Workers' Union, China Merchants Bureau Fifth Wharf Workers' Union, Huining Sojourners Association, Calligraphy and Fan Workers' Union, French Concession Water and Electricity Workers' Union, Pharmaceutical Industry Union, Chinese and Foreign Cloth Industry Workers' Union, Huacheng Tobacco Factory Workers' Union, Tea Industry Workers' Union, Sanyou Industrial Co. Workers' Union, and Steamboat Wood Industry Workers' Union. (5) Resolved to send five representatives to petition the municipal government. Cai Xiaohe, Wang Changyuan, Hu Bihang, Wang Yongliang, and Zhang Shenzhi were elected as representatives. (6) Send a letter to Du Yuesheng, a Chinese director of the French Concession and chairman of the Chinese Directors Association, requesting him to uphold justice and promptly negotiate seriously with the French authorities to achieve the goals. The original letter is recorded below. To: Du Yuesheng, Dear Sir, Xin Dingxiang, a sampanman, was beaten and drowned by a sailor from the French Navy's warship Walter Kochsha for demanding ferry fare. Since the incident occurred, more than a month has passed. Due to the obstruction of unequal treaties, although our association has been running around and appealing, the other party has not shown any remorse or sincerity in resolving the matter. The grievance has not been redressed, and the people's feelings are indignant. You, sir, are a Chinese director of the French Municipal Council, a leader of the merchants, and your chivalrous reputation has long been known far and wide. You must have deep sympathy for this tragedy. Xin Dingxiang's father is old and his family is poor, and his pregnant wife has suffered a tragic death, leaving them destitute. Deliberating the circumstances, they are truly pitiful. The murderer is still at large, which is deeply hateful. We respectfully ask you, sir, to uphold your long-standing ambition to suppress the strong and support the weak, to advocate for justice and fairness, and to promptly negotiate seriously to achieve the desired goals, so that a satisfactory resolution can be reached. The rights of the nation are deeply reliant on this. Please consider and respond to this. Respectfully, The Xin Case Support Association.

Yancheng Woman Kidnapped and Brought to Shanghai by Bandits

Raped and Taken as Wife

Two Bandits Simultaneously Detained

A woman named Wang Xiaomei from Yancheng was kidnapped for ransom by Ma Yuren's subordinates in August of the lunar calendar this year. Her family did not care because they had no money to redeem her. On October 1st, the bandits Chen Zhaotai and Liu Guren abducted Wang and brought her to Shanghai, residing on Hanzhong Road in Zhabei, where they raped and occupied her. Yesterday, the hostage Wang Xiaomei took advantage of the fact that nobody was guarding her during Liu's wedding and escaped to her uncle's house, where she reported the case to the police, who arrested the two bandits Chen and Liu and detained them in the Fourth District Public Security Bureau of Zhabei. The details are as follows:

Kidnapping for Ransom: Wang Xiaomei, 23 years old, originally lived in Yancheng. This year, due to Ma Yuren's rebellion in Jiangbei, she took refuge in Shagou City. On August 17th of the lunar calendar, Ma's bandits again robbed in Shagou, gathering more than 2,000 people, robbing houses and looting shops, and kidnapping hundreds of women, including Wang Xiaomei. She was taken away by the bandits Chen Zhaoxiong and Liu Guren, who sent a letter to her family demanding 1,000 yuan for ransom. Wang's family was destitute and unable to raise the money, so they had to let it go. On October 1st, Chen and Liu took the stolen furniture and other items with Wang Xiaomei to Shanghai, first residing in Tangjiawan, Ximen, and later moving to No. 51 Hanzhong Li, Hanzhong Road, Zhabei. Chen Zhaoxiong also raped Wang Xiaomei and took her as his wife.

Escaping During the Opportunity: Liu Zhaoxiong, 29 years old, was not yet married. Yesterday was an auspicious day for him to marry his child bride, Chen. His family was quite busy, so no one paid attention to Wang Xiaomei's actions. Before lunch, Wang Xiaomei took advantage of the opportunity while emptying the chamber pot to escape secretly and go to her uncle Wang Yaoting's house, where she told him about being abducted and raped. He immediately reported to the police, who arrested Chen Zhaoxiong and Liu Guren, along with suspects Gu Kegang and Zhao Deji, and detained them in the Fourth District Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Strict Handling by the Bureau: After arriving at the bureau, Wang Xiaomei recounted the details of being kidnapped and abducted. When questioned, the defendant Chen Zhaoxiong denied the incident, claiming that he was a soldier under Ma Yuren for eight months and was ordered to rob and kidnap people in Shagou. He met Wang Xiaomei on the boat but did not demand ransom or rape her. Liu Guren stated that he did not know Chen Zhaoxiong and only met him on a boat in Dongtai on September 9th of the lunar calendar. He did not rob or kidnap any women. Since Wang Xiaomei had no place to live, he invited her to stay at his house temporarily. Suspect Gu Kegang stated that Liu Guren was the nephew of his wife's ex-husband, and he brought Chen Zhaoxiong and Wang Xiaomei to live in Shanghai. He did not know that they were bandits. According to the household registration police report, Chen and Liu moved from Tangjiawan to Hanzhong Road, Zhabei on November 15. The householder was Meng Bugao. Chen Zhaoxiong was Meng's cousin, and Liu was the householder's brother-in-law. His wife was Wang. After verifying the statements, District Chief Jin determined that the two bandits Chen and Liu were guilty of kidnapping and raping women, and the crimes were heinous. He ordered them to be sent to the judicial section for strict handling.

Tragedy Under Car Wheels

One Dead, Two Injured

Rickshaw Puller Loses Both Legs: A certain Westerner residing on Jiangwan Road employed a rickshaw puller named Gu Luping, 25 years old. Last night at 7:30 PM, his employer instructed him to take a guest to the ball field entrance on Nanjing Road. Upon reaching the destination, the guest alighted and departed. Gu then pulled his empty rickshaw to return. Not far along, another guest loudly hailed a rickshaw to the shooting range. Gu, thinking it was a convenient route home, and why not earn a little extra money, greeted him with a smile. He carried the guest speeding north. Who knew that good things often have setbacks? While traveling on Laobazi Road north of Sichuan Road, there were several cars ahead winding like long snakes. Unexpectedly, a public bus, driven by a Russian driver of the number 340, came from behind. The Russian, excessively drunk, drove erratically, ignoring everything. He charged straight ahead, and with a loud crash, a major disaster occurred. Gu's rickshaw was struck onto the curb. Fortunately, the passenger was alert, leaped down, and escaped unharmed, suffering only minor abrasions. The rickshaw puller, Gu Luping, fell to the ground, breaking both legs. A car parked on the side of the road suffered minor damage to its front. Two other rickshaws were also affected. As for the struck rickshaw, it was smashed to bits and beyond repair. Seeing the disaster he had caused, the Russian driver stepped on the gas and fled. Officer number 1053 blew his whistle frantically, summoning nearby officers to intercept him. Initially, the Russian looked fierce, as if to punch the officer, but as onlookers gathered and shouted, he dared not make a sound. The officer recorded the number, and the car was allowed to proceed. The injured were taken to Tongren Hospital.

Old Woman Bloodied Beyond Recognition: An old woman from Jiangbei, Yang Wen, over sixty years of age, residing in a bungalow on Baoxing Road, Zhabei, intended to go to the Nan Shi 16 Pu last evening around 6:00 PM to take a boat back to her hometown. She had just reached the entrance of the park on the Outer White Bridge when a public bus driven by a Russian driver came towards her. Due to her age and frailty, she could not avoid it and was knocked to the ground. The wheel ran over her body, breaking her skull. She was bloodied beyond recognition, a horrifying sight. Officer number 1229, hearing the alarm, arrived at the scene and had the injured woman taken to Tongren Hospital for treatment. However, her injuries were too severe, and she died half an hour after arriving.

Apprentice Severely Injured: Sun Xizhen, a police officer of the second squad of the sixth district of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, received a report around 3:00 PM the day before yesterday that a student, about fifteen or sixteen years old, riding a bicycle on the Puxi Road of Xujiahui, west of Shanghai, in front of the Yuantai Rice Shop at number 22, traveling south, was suddenly struck from behind by a business car with municipal license number 4177, causing a head injury. The injury was quite severe. Officer Sun rushed to the scene and took the person and car involved to the station. Director Liu then dispatched Inspector Yuan to inspect the scene of the accident. At the time, a rickshaw was passing on the injured person's left. The road was narrow, and it bumped the bicycle, causing the person and bicycle to fall to the right. The car that caused the accident came along shortly after and, because it was traveling too fast, could not brake in time, causing a head injury and a fracture of the zygomatic bone on the left temple. The victim could not speak. At the time, a car was hired to take the injured person to the Red Cross for treatment on Haig Road, and witness Xia Guangxin was taken to the station for questioning. According to the car driver, Zhu Shangfu, 34 years old, from Ningbo, was a driver for the Billem Motor Company on Broadway. He had been there for less than two months and had not yet obtained a Chinese license. Today, he was driving a municipal license number 4177 car to the Catholic Church to drop off a guest. When he arrived in front of number 22 Puxi Road, a student riding a bicycle in front of him, for some reason, fell to the right. Because the bicycle was so close, he could not stop in time, causing the student's head to be injured. According to witness Xia Guangxin, from Huizhou, the situation at the time of the accident was not clear. However, he saw the injured student being dragged from under the car wheels. Afterward, he helped the police officer take him to the hospital. The rest he did not know. Shortly afterward, the injured person's brother-in-law, Shu Changshun, came to the station, claiming to be from Ningbo, currently residing at number 1 Yipin Lane, Bailinan Road. The injured person's name was Chen Shouchun, 15 years old, my younger cousin, currently studying at Xujiahui Public School at the Catholic Church. His parents are both in his hometown. As for what to do, I cannot make a decision. I must wait for my parents-in-law to come to Shanghai. Director Liu then prepared a document sending the car driver Zhu Shangfu, witness Xia Guangxin, along with car number 4177, to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for questioning.

Municipal Public Works Bureau to Issue New Small Car Licenses

To Begin Processing from December 1st

The Municipal Public Works Bureau issued a notice yesterday stating, regarding the notice: Upon inspection, the issuance of 20-year small car licenses for this city will begin on December 1st of this year. At the same time, new numbers will be recompiled and license plates issued. All small car owners are requested to push their vehicles to the nearby bureau's vehicle office before paying the December monthly fee to restamp the steel seal and obtain new license plates and 20-year licenses (valid until the end of June of the 10th year). Pay a fee of 12 cents for the license exchange. Those who have not previously received a license plate should pay a deposit of 30 cents. Those who have already received an old license plate but have not exchanged it by December 15th will have their license number revoked and the original deposit forfeited. This notice is hereby issued for general knowledge.

Airplanes Assist Water Police in Suppressing Pirates Outside Wusong Port

Pirates outside Wusong Port have become rampant. Recently, there was a fight between pirate leaders, such that pirates can be found almost everywhere on the seas. Zhang Han, the director of the fourth district of the Wusong Water Police, has repeatedly ordered the 16th, 17th, and 18th squads under his command to search and suppress them. However, because the coastal areas outside the port are mostly remote, with numerous harbors, and shifting sands appear and disappear unpredictably, suppression is difficult to achieve. Therefore, the pirates have not been completely suppressed to this day. The day before yesterday, Director Zhang, together with the county magistrates of Tongzhou, Chongming, Hai'an, and Qidong counties, held a meeting and decided to request the Civil Affairs Department of the Jiangsu Provincial Government to forward a request to the Central Government to quickly dispatch airplanes to assist in the suppression so that the pirates can be suppressed as soon as possible to avoid future troubles. It is learned that the Central Government has approved the request, and airplanes will be dispatched to assist in the suppression in the coming days.

He Gengxing Continues to be Accused

According to the plaintiff's complaint, He Gengxing, in addition to opening Hongyu and Huiyu Hardware Stores, also jointly and solely owned Yuyuan Money Shop, Tian'an Rubber Company, Qianxun Pawnshop, and Shou Xing Real Estate Company. Hongyu and Huiyu had overdraft transactions with the plaintiffs. On May 24, He Gengxing and Ma Changjia absconded with funds, owing the plaintiffs a large sum. They made arrangements in advance and filed for bankruptcy with the French Consulate, which appointed an accountant to liquidate. When the plaintiffs checked the accounts, the Hongyu ledger contained an entry on May 23 stating that 150,000 taels of gold were received from Youji and 150,000 taels were paid to He Gengxing, and the handwriting was altered. Upon closer inspection, the "Geng" character was changed from "Shou." When checking He Gengxing's account, there was also such a record, and other accounts were also inconsistent. Zhao Guangzu Unwilling to Divorce

Files a Plea with the Special District Court

After Zhao Tan Meiying filed a petition for divorce from Zhao Guangzu with the Special District Court, it was heard that Zhao Guangzu had filed a plea with the Special District Court, hoping for reconciliation. The plea is recorded as follows: "Civil Plea Document." Pleader: Zhao Guangzu, Agent: Lawyer Gao Shuo, Plaintiff: Zhao Tan Meiying. Regarding the case of Zhao Tan Meiying's lawsuit for divorce, the occurrence of this case is directly a misfortune for the family and indirectly an impact on society. The trial was hastily conducted the other day, and a declaration of the conclusion of the debate was made. Fearing that the lower circumstances could not be conveyed to the higher authorities, I will add additional reasons. The plea is as follows: (1) The doctor's certificate is not credible. Upon inspection, there was no quarreling that day, how could there be beating? If it happened, the plaintiff would have deliberately filed a lawsuit and could have directly reported the arrest, how could she calmly seek medical treatment? Furthermore, according to the doctor's rules, a blank form is used to create a medical certificate, how can a random letter of stationery be used for proof? (2) The witness Gao is bribed. The defendant had stated that the Gao Zhang called by the plaintiff to the court had repeatedly wanted to quit and refused to testify. The court did not adopt this but still ordered the witness to appear and state. When Gao Zhang first stated, she said that she heard them arguing and did not remember whether they hit each other. The plaintiff was standing nearby at that time and scolded the witness. The presiding judge of the court made a remark of reprimand. Afterward, the witness complied with the plaintiff's wishes and made a statement, which clearly shows that the witness was bribed and cannot be used as evidence. (3) The two letters are casual writings between husband and wife and were before the Meifei case was filed. The defendant had previously been in love with Meifei, and there were often quarrels between husband and wife, so there were casual writings on May 12, 7, and 18. After the plaintiff came forward to file a lawsuit (in late July) and the relationship with Meifei was severed, the defendant never had any licentious facts. If the plaintiff wanted to break away from the husband-wife relationship with the defendant, why did she come forward to tell about Meifei's matter? The defendant has obeyed, changed his ways, and corrected his mistakes. How can the plaintiff take the facts from the past as a reason for divorce? It is important to investigate the key to this case. (1) Were the previous two divorce letters before or after the plaintiff filed a lawsuit against Meifei? (2) Is the defendant still involved in flirtatious activities, so as to estimate whether there is a basis for divorce? As for casual writings between husband and wife, there are constant things that are not enough to be believed. On October 4 of this year, the plaintiff also had a handwritten letter stating, "If Guangzu has an accident, Meiying is willing to use a glass coffin worth 750 taels to collect Guangzu." The original letter is also attached. If so, can the defendant be accused of inciting suicide against the plaintiff? These casual writings are originally absurd matters of the boudoir and are not sufficient to provide evidence in court. (4) The witness should be added. Upon investigation, the organization of the defendant's family is not as simple as the plaintiff described. There is also brother Zhao Guangde living in the same family. Instead of taking evidence from ignorant and illiterate maids who are easily bribed, it is better to interview co-residents and neighbors to get the truth. The defendant previously requested in court that fear of language barriers not be granted. I hereby apply for additional transmission to show fairness. In general, the world is getting worse, etiquette is sinking, and young men and women are often easily tempted by the outside world. After the defendant was sued by the plaintiff for the Meifei case, he was deeply motivated and wished to make amends, abandon evil and return to righteousness, and be kind and loving to each other for a long-term marriage. Unexpectedly, the plaintiff suddenly had a different intention and changed her original intention, which is a great misfortune in life. If what the plaintiff accuses is a recent fact, then there is still a reason for returning, but it is self-inflicted. The only thing is the past, which is the fact before the defendant repented (the matter before the plaintiff sued Meifei). It is not right for the plaintiff to change her mind and it is a manifestation of the instability of young people's minds. According to Article 677 of the Civil Procedure Law, in a lawsuit for divorce and a lawsuit for husband and wife to live together, the court shall advise reconciliation at any time during the oral debate. Article 678 of the Civil Procedure Law states that in a lawsuit for divorce and a lawsuit for husband and wife to live together, if the court believes that the parties have hope of harmony, it may order the suspension of the proceedings for a period of up to one year, but only once, etc. The plaintiff in this case does not have very important facts that cannot be cohabitated with the defendant, and the facts are all previous events of the defendant. The plaintiff and the defendant have both admitted that they regret their previous actions, so they jointly sued Meifei for fraud in late July of this year. The plaintiff is the plaintiff in the case, and the defendant is the witness in the case. There is a case to be checked. Now, the plaintiff raises the past for no reason, which is not contradictory. It must be seduced or for a moment of anger. I beg your court to allow a re-hearing and order a limited time to try to reconcile in order to restore the marriage and maintain ethics. The defendant's two brothers share property, and the defendant's common copper seal are in the plaintiff's possession. I should ask that it be ordered to be temporarily handed over to prevent accidents. Combined statement, respectfully to the Shanghai Special District Court. Witness Zhao Guangde, 17 years old, Shanghai, resident of the residence at No. 1100 Huade Road, student, neighbor surnamed Yao, resident of No. 320 Huade Road, former co-resident.

Concealing a Woman from a Good Family

Failure to Succeed and Extortion of Money

Yu A'si from Jiading, fourteen years old, was given to the Li family from the same village as a daughter when she was young, named Yue Bao. A'si is quite beautiful and dresses similarly to a female student in the inland. Her father's name is Mengfu, and he is a local guard in his hometown. Her grandfather, A'chun, works in the Caojiadu Fire Brigade in this city. Recently, her neighbor, Aunt Zhang Zhao, is blind and came to Shanghai for medical treatment accompanied by her son, Guohua. A'si admired the prosperous markets of Shanghai and had never been there before. Taking advantage of this opportunity, she also came to Shanghai and stayed at the Huian Hotel on Zhejiang Road. By chance, Li Kou and Qu Longchang from Tongzhou had worked as partners in a Jiading rosewood workshop, so they knew Zhang. By chance, they met Zhang on the road and, after exchanging greetings, gathered at the hotel to talk. Li and Qu saw that A'si was very beautiful and had malicious intentions. They pretended to go to Caojiadu to find her grandfather, using the opportunity to entice A'si to a bungalow near the San Wan Factory in Lujiazui, Pudong. A'si saw that the place she arrived at was not like the fire brigade and that her grandfather was never seen, so she knew that Li and Qu were not well-intentioned and covered her face and cried. A police officer saw this and asked questions. Li and Qu saw that things were not going well and slipped away. A'si was taken to the Third District Police Station by the police. After the district chief understood the reason, he ordered her to stay in the district temporarily and wait for her family to claim her. Li and Qu saw that their plan had failed and were frustrated. However, they were unwilling to give up, so they planned to have Qu return to Pudong alone and contact Zhang Guohua, demanding 150 yuan to return the person. Zhang was suffering from the loss of A'si and became even more angry when he heard this. He twisted Qu to the French Concession Police Station and requested that A'si be recovered. Qu confessed that A'si was hidden in Pudong by them. The police station ruled that the case occurred in the Chinese territory and transferred the plaintiff and defendant to the first division of the second district. After questioning by the director, it was ruled that Qu concealed a woman from a good family, failed, and tried to extort money. His crime was inescapable, so he was ordered to be sent to the General Bureau for disposal. After this case occurred, it was reported in the newspaper yesterday. A'si's grandfather, Qian A'chun, read it and came to Pudong yesterday to report to the third district, confirming that A'si was his granddaughter. At the same time, the district chief ruled that the principal offender of the abduction had surrendered himself and was now detained at the General Bureau awaiting investigation, so he also sent the grandfather and granddaughter to the bureau for joint interrogation.

Yan Hongde and Zhang Clash, Accusing Each Other

Involving Schoolteacher Yang Shuhui

Yan Hongde, a 35-year-old man from Yangzhou, resides at No. 3273, Yaozu Lane, Wuzhou Road, Youheng Road, Hongkou East. He used to work as a foreman. In the eighth year of the Republic of China, he married Zhang Jinbiao's younger sister, Zhang, from Gaoyou, as his concubine. The following year, they had a daughter named Suzhen, who is now ten years old. Initially, they lived separately in Yongkang Lane, Hujia Wood Bridge. Later, Zhang's brother, Zhang Jinbiao, sued Yan in the local court, accusing him of bigamy. However, Zhang appeared in court and stated that what was done was done and she willingly retreated to the position of concubine, leading to the withdrawal of the case. They lived peacefully without incident. At the beginning of this month, Yan Hongde hired lawyer Fan Ming to file a private prosecution in the criminal division of the local court, stating that his concubine, Zhang, was secretly associating with Yang Shuhui, a schoolteacher living nearby. He saw that Zhang was outwardly attentive, so he suspected nothing. The year before last, Zhang asked to move back home, but Yan was afraid that his wife and concubine living together would be inappropriate, so he refused. Subsequently, Zhang repeatedly pleaded, so he moved back home last year. Until now, the relationship between the wife and concubine has been harmonious. Unexpectedly, Zhang secretly associated with Yang Shuhui. Although the neighbors knew, they kept it secret. Zhang's intentions were insidious. She gradually moved out of the house a total of 480 silver dollars in savings and clothing, etc. On the second of this month, Zhang used the excuse of going out to join a rotating credit association and never returned. After Yan discovered this, he checked the clothes and found nothing left. Only then did friends tell him the truth. Yan went to Yongkang Lane, where Yang Shuhui lived, to inquire. According to the neighbors, he had already moved to Tianbao Road, Xiangyan Bridge, and was living with someone named Shen. Yan went to the address to inquire. The neighbors all knew that a woman and a young girl were living in the house with Yang, coming and going together. Zhang absconded with the money and took the girl with her. Her intentions were clever and her methods were too ruthless. After more than ten years as husband and wife, this is the result. If he were to tolerate this and not speak out, how would the good customs of society be maintained? Therefore, he filed the lawsuit. Zhang, hired lawyer Jiang Rong to send a letter to Yan Hongde, stating that she had left home to live elsewhere because she could not stand the abuse, and intended to sever the relationship, requesting a compensation of 1,000 silver dollars, and 1,400 silver dollars for the girl's education, etc. This case was summoned for trial, but only the plaintiff appeared in court. As a result, the private prosecution was rejected and the case was transferred to the prosecutor's office for investigation and handling. A few days ago, the police station of the Fifth District, Second Precinct arrested Yan Zhang and Yang Shuhui one after another and transferred them to the detective team. The team sent Zhang to the Third Section, which transferred her to the local court for interrogation. After the interrogation, she was ordered to return and await instructions. Now, Yan Hongde has submitted a supplementary lawsuit to the court, stating that the defendant Yang Shuhui is currently being detained by the detective team, and that Yan Zhang (28 years old) has been detained by the detective team and brought to the court. He requested that the case be strictly investigated, and also filed a civil suit, seeking a public prosecution to investigate the stolen clothing, silver dollars, and the girl's matter. This case was filed on the eighth of this month. The court ruled on the thirteenth of this month to reject it, notifying the prosecutor's office, stating that it had already been reported. He received a summons from the prosecutor of the court yesterday, scheduling a hearing (today) for legal interrogation. After Zhang was seduced by Yang Shuhui into adultery, Zhang became restless. Starting in February of this year, she instigated Zhang to tell him that she wanted to borrow several hundred silver dollars, otherwise she would threaten him with a pistol. Then she encouraged Zhang to move back home, so that she could take the opportunity to steal property. Because he was employed by others, leaving early and returning late, he had no way of knowing. On the third of this month, Zhang left and did not return, and all the clothes were stolen. Afterwards, someone witnessed Yang Shuhui and Zhang talking privately, which was not the first time. From this, clues could be found. At that time, in addition to reporting to the Public Security Bureau's detective team for investigation, he also filed a lawsuit with the court, requesting the police to arrest them for investigation. Since the private prosecution has been rejected, he pleads directly to the prosecutor's office to investigate according to the law, file a public prosecution, and strictly punish them.

Third Call for Funds for Shangyu Embankment Project

The Shangyu embankment project, which has been underway for some time since fellow villagers in Shanghai raised funds to start construction, requires approximately 80,000 yuan in labor and materials. The amount of donations received is not substantial, and the banks of the Cao'e River have recently collapsed again. If no measures are taken to repair them, the flood will be severe. Therefore, a third letter of solicitation was issued. The letter states: "We are writing to inform you that this embankment project relies entirely on the initiating gentlemen who gathered comrades, made great vows, and started construction. The estimated cost of labor and materials is approximately 80,000 yuan. It was agreed to raise funds separately and proceed. Recently, the embankment project has begun, and funds are urgently needed like stars in the night sky. The total amount of donations received is only over 30,000 yuan, which is far from sufficient. If it is interrupted midway, it will be more dangerous than the original earthen embankment. Thinking of this, we cannot sleep or eat in peace. We can only ask you again to make every effort to find a way, either to donate generously or to raise funds widely, to meet the urgent needs, so that we can take advantage of this winter season when the tides are smaller to complete the project. This is our sincere prayer." (The rest is omitted)

Land Without People

Where does the opium come from?

Let's send the stolen goods to the bureau

Fu Jixiang, patrol captain of the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau's Water Patrol Team, and detectives Liu Changrui and Yang Chunting, while patrolling the river near the Datong Wharf at around 12:00 noon yesterday, noticed the Hua'an steamship docked there. They immediately boarded the ship to conduct an inspection. They then went to the steerage section of the ship and found a bag in the luggage of a recruit of the 56th Division of the National Revolutionary Army. Upon inspection, they found three packages of opium, totaling more than sixty taels, and an iron box containing eleven opium pills and a box of opium paste. After inquiring, no one claimed ownership. So they took the team away. Later, Wang Shenwu, a platoon leader of the division, surrendered to the team. When Xu, the chief of the team, questioned him, he said that more than 500 recruits had been recruited this time and were traveling to Shanghai on the ship before transferring to Fujian Province. He did not know who brought the opium. He ordered that a report be prepared with the seized evidence and submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau for review and handling.

Tao Dongfu's Tragic Death is Pitiful

Tao Dongfu, a 53-year-old man from Nanjing, worked as a foreman at the Shunchang copper shop on Jinlong Street in the Public Concession. On the afternoon of the 22nd, he went to a copper shop near Xiaonanmen to pick up a basket of copperware to bring back to the shop. At 5:50 p.m., while heading north on Zilai Street in the French Concession towards Avenue Edward VII, he was struck by a car driven by a driver from the Tan Le Motor Company (license number 7827). Tao was unable to avoid it and was knocked down by the car's rear fender, suffering head injuries. The police who arrived at the scene recorded the license number and sent Tao to Renji Hospital. They then returned to the police station to report to the head of the police. Tao died from his injuries without effective treatment at 11:00 p.m. the day before yesterday. The hospital notified the police station, and the body was taken to the Tongren Fuyuan Hall autopsy room to await examination. Because the name and address of Tao were unknown at the time, it was impossible to find his family. Yesterday, the Vehicle Department of the French Police Station reported to Judge Zhu of the French Court, who came to the scene and confirmed that the deceased had died from injuries sustained in a car accident. He ordered that photos be taken and the body be kept by the court, pending identification by family members. The defendant driver was released on bail. If no family members come forward within six months, the case will be dismissed. Later, the deceased's companions identified the body at the autopsy room and notified the family to collect it. It is reported that the deceased had parents, a wife, and children who depended on him for support. Now that he has suffered this tragic misfortune, the family's livelihood will be difficult from now on.

Local News

National Tongji University President Hu Shuhua Resubmits Resignation

President Hu Shuhua of National Tongji University previously resigned from his post due to financial difficulties, but the Ministry of Education retained him. Now, because the school is extremely difficult to maintain, he has resubmitted his resignation to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Education. His original submission states:

Submitted for the purpose of explaining the difficult situation, requesting review and approval of resignation. I, Shuhua, was honored to be appointed to the position of president more than a year ago. Recalling the beginning of my appointment, I privately wished to devote all my energy to the task, in order to live up to the Party and the country's intention to cultivate talent. However, in recent years, funding has been exhausted, coupled with the school's unique history, and the difficulties have been great. Only 30% to 40% of my efforts have been devoted to academic achievements, while 60% to 70% of my energy has been spent on dealing with requests for payment. I am worried day and night. I feel that I can no longer help with the difficulties, and I should give way to a more capable person to avoid making mistakes. At the beginning of this academic year, I repeatedly submitted my resignation, but it was not approved. I勉力 support until now, but the difficulties have doubled. I would like to present the current situation of the school in detail, respectfully requesting your review. The school was founded by Germans. In the fifth year of the Republic of China, it was taken over and run independently. Until the spring of the sixteenth year, it was affected by military events, and the school lacked leadership. It relied on borrowing to survive. In addition, the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office stopped issuing subsidies in the winter of the seventeenth year. By the time Shuhua arrived at the school on June 20th of the eighteenth year and took over, there were already heavy debts and a towering debt. It is estimated that it owed German commercial groups and Puel Yangxing and other loans, totaling 118,400 silver dollars, unpaid salaries to German teachers and staff of 73,900 silver dollars, and overdrafts from banks of 30,000 silver dollars, totaling more than 220,000 silver dollars. The school has no foundation or assets to draw on. Although efforts have been made to reorganize, there is no way to make up for the huge losses. Moreover, the school has a special situation that is very different from other schools. The professors are all Germans, and they are full-time teachers with many teaching hours, so their salaries are higher than normal. The medical and engineering departments both place a heavy emphasis on practical training, which is very costly. The monthly expenses are 34,725 silver dollars. The salaries of teachers and staff in the university, middle school, and affiliated mechanic school total more than 21,000 silver dollars. The factory, the anatomy research institute, and the physiology research institute spend approximately 5,600 silver dollars on practical training. Equipment and administrative expenses are only 7,900 silver dollars. Therefore, monthly expenses always exceed the budget. Efforts are made to make ends meet. In the eighteenth year, more than 70,000 silver dollars of old bonds were sold, and more than 20,000 silver dollars were saved from regular expenses, so a total of 53,000 silver dollars were used to repay old debts and interest. A high-voltage electricity testing laboratory and a cast iron chemical testing laboratory were built for the practical training needs of the engineering school. The physiology research institute of the medical school had been planned for several years. It was only at the beginning of this year that funds were allocated, and with the support of the Cultural Foundation Committee, the building was fortunately completed. However, all the internal equipment is still empty. As for the establishment of a science school to complete the university organization, although it has been approved, there is no way to raise funds. Although Baolong Hospital is a place for students to practice, it is not a long-term solution to live under someone else's roof. Therefore, it seems that a teaching hospital should be established on its own. Most of the medical school teachers work at Baolong Hospital. Although they do not receive salaries for teaching, their sense of responsibility is also reduced. Therefore, in the nineteenth year's budget, Shuhua requested that all medical school teachers be paid a salary. Now, the funds received are still based on the seventeenth year's budget. All kinds of improvement plans have become bubbles. Now, since the beginning of this year, five months have passed, and only 10,000 silver dollars have been issued for July's expenses. Previously, due to the sharp fall in silver prices and the surge in marks, it has been approved to subsidize German professors a total of 3,720 silver dollars per month, but only July and August have been paid. Therefore, German professors are dissatisfied because old debts have not been repaid and new debts have increased. At first, they complained, but recently they have questioned harshly. These professors all signed contracts for several years when they came to China, so they brought their families and stayed here. Once their salaries are in arrears, it is difficult for them to maintain their lives. This is also the truth. Moreover, the regulations and credit are at stake, and they cannot be satisfied with empty words. As for the practical training fees for the medical and engineering departments, they are indispensable every day. In ordinary times, if there is a lack of practical materials, the German professors will refuse to teach. Their sense of responsibility is certainly understandable. In this time of economic hardship, it is even more impossible to deal with. Moreover, all the water and electricity for the school are supplied by the practical training factory. Now, the factory has no funds to purchase the materials needed. In the future, not only will the professors strike, but the factory may also stop working. I am incompetent and have no way to make up for the deficiencies. If this continues, I will not be able to sleep or eat in peace. From morning to night, those who come to the president's office are either demanding payment of old debts or chasing unpaid salaries. I have no time to think about academic matters. This violates my original intention and I am afraid of making mistakes. I do not want the school's long history to be interrupted in the middle. It is appropriate to present the difficult situation in detail. I humbly request that you approve my resignation from the position of president and appoint a capable person to replace me, so that he can save the school from danger and promote school affairs. I await your orders with utmost anxiety. In addition to submitting separately, I respectfully submit this to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Education.

Last Night's West Youth Basketball Game: John Wins Over McKinley

John 34... McKinley 23

Xia Guang 23... Nan Feng 14

丨There are six Group A teams competing tonight丨

The West Youth Basketball Association held Group A and B matches last night, starting at 7:50 PM. The results were: (1) Group B, Xia Guang defeated Nan Feng 23 to 14; (2) Group A, John defeated McKinley 34 to 23. John's victory was actually quite precarious. Chen Xianglong was in danger of being ejected in the first half due to four fouls, but fortunately, he fought hard in the end. Hou Xuemin made many shots, securing the win. Details are as follows:

Xia Guang Wins Over Nan Feng (Group B)

丨23 to 14丨

The first match, Xia Guang versus Nan Feng, was a decent performance. Both sides moved quite clearly, but their ball skills seemed less refined, and they lacked confidence in shooting, resulting in few points. Xia Guang took an early lead of 8 to 2. Nan Feng worked hard to catch up, ending the first half at 9 to 6, with Xia Guang leading by three points. Starting in the second half, Nan Feng's Guo Jiming and Xin Dingkui added three points, tying the game at 9 to 9. However, after that, Xia Guang's momentum suddenly surged. Chen Zhaoyu circled under the basket, lively and extraordinary, repeatedly making shots and earning much applause. Although Nan Feng tried to counterattack, their inaccurate shots made it difficult to score. Xia Guang, relying on Chen Zhaoyu's efforts, secured the final victory at 23 to 14. In the second half, Xia Guang scored a total of 14 points, all by Chen Zhaoyu alone, which was no easy feat. Referee: Tafors.

Xia Guang Fouls and Points, Nan Feng Fouls and Points: Right Forward Kang Yuefa 3 fouls, 1 point. Right Forward Ma Youcheng 1 foul, 2 points. Left Forward Zhao Jiabin 1 foul, 0 points. Right Forward Guo Jiming 0 fouls, 1 point. Left Forward Chen Zhaoyu 1 foul, 14 points. Left Forward Zhou Chaojie 2 fouls, 6 points. Center Cai Yan 0 fouls, 3 points. Center Li Mingxiong 1 foul, 4 points. Right Guard Hu Mingxin 1 foul, 2 points. Right Guard Xin Dingkui 1 foul, 1 point. Left Guard Ren Jiexing 1 foul, 3 points. Left Guard Chen Yongkang 1 foul, 0 points. Total: 7 fouls, 23 points. Total: 6 fouls, 14 points. First half: Xia Guang 9 points, Nan Feng 6 points. Second half: Xia Guang 14 points, Nan Feng 8 points.

John vs. McKinley (Group A)

丨34 to 23丨

The second match was Group A, John versus McKinley. The battle was fierce, and the situation seemed quite even. At the start, McKinley's Si Huoyuan scored, opening the record. John missed both free throws. After a long stalemate, Diao Youdao tossed a ball backward into the basket, and Chen Xianglong jumped up and tapped it in. These two miraculous shots were highly praised by the spectators. John then took a lead of 4 to 2. However, John's defense was quite lax; two players often stayed on the same line, allowing opponents to break through. Fortunately, McKinley's shots were inaccurate, keeping John safe. John coordinated their offense, and Hou Xuemin, like a butterfly picking flowers, was lively and agile, continuing to score. Lin Zejun also added a point. McKinley quickly chased after them, making the score 10 to 9. Suddenly, Chen Xianglong made a one-handed shot. McKinley's Meng Si committed two unpenalized movements and was stolen two points. Su Tai made a free throw, making the score quite close (12 to 12). John attacked with all their might. Hou Xuemin made two corner shots, taking the lead again at 16 to 12. McKinley refused to show weakness, rallying their spirits and striving to retaliate. Disaster struck John when center Chen Xianglong was dismissed with four fouls, weakening their strength. Fortunately, they defended hard. John still won the first half with a score of 19 to 13.

Starting in the second half, neither side yielded, and the situation was quite tense. However, John never lagged behind, but McKinley followed closely, with only a slight difference. The closest the score came was 23 to 21, only two points apart, making it very precarious. John then paused the game to reorganize their forces, and their momentum suddenly surged. The spectators were also energized. Hou Xuemin moved under the basket, unpredictable, repeatedly scoring and receiving great applause from the audience. In the end, John won with a score of 34 to 23. Hou Xuemin alone scored 20 points, making a great contribution. Referee: Brand.

Record of the Shanghai Basketball League Committee

The Shanghai Basketball League, sponsored by the China National Sports Federation, held its first committee meeting at the Da Zhonghua Restaurant at 6 PM the day before yesterday, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. The details are recorded below. Those present on the day included Ling Xitao, Zhang Guoxun, Rong Qizhao, Xu Zhendong, Ma Detai, and Zhou Jiaqi (secretary). Xu Zhendong was elected as the chairman of the committee, and they passed the constitution, discussed competition matters, and resolved: (1) The registration for the women's league has ended, but only four teams have joined: Zhenru, Yaguang, Liangjiang A, and Liangjiang B. The number of teams is too small, reducing the interest in the competition. Therefore, it was decided to extend the registration period by one week (ending on the 30th) to solicit other teams to join. The competition will begin on December 3rd. (2) January 3rd of the 20th year is set as the start date for the men's basketball league. Registration will begin on December 10th of this year and end on the 20th.

Attached: Constitution of the Women's Basketball League

1. This league is sponsored by the China National Sports Federation and is named the Shanghai Women's Basketball League.

2. Any amateur organization in Shanghai that has a formal request and is approved by this league, and has paid the membership fee of ten yuan, is a formal member.

3. This league has a committee to handle all administrative matters in the league.

4. This league has one secretary, concurrently held by a staff member of the federation.

5. At the beginning of each season, members participating in the competition should submit a list of players participating in the competition to the secretariat within the specified date and pay a registration fee of five yuan.

6. Each team is limited to 14 registered players. Once registered, no additions or changes are allowed. Unregistered players are not allowed to participate in the competition.

7. Each team will be issued player cards by this league. These cards are only valid for admission to various competitions within this league.

8. Competition referees are hired by this league.

9. Competition rules are implemented according to the Far Eastern Games women's basketball rules.

10. All competitions are held at the China Basketball Hall.

11. If a member or player violates the constitution of this league, the committee will determine the punishment method: (A) Warning, (B) Fine, (C) Suspension of the member or player's eligibility to compete, (D) Revocation of membership or individual eligibility.

12. The scheduled competition dates and times cannot be changed. If the league notifies a change of date due to unforeseen circumstances, this does not apply.

13. If a change of date is necessary due to unavoidable accidents, the league should be requested for permission two days before the competition.

14. Teams that do not arrive within ten minutes of the scheduled competition time will be considered as forfeiting. If both sides do not arrive, both will be considered as forfeiting. Forfeiting twice will result in the cancellation of their membership. Unless there is a concrete guarantee approved by this league, they will not be allowed to rejoin in the next session.

15. If a member withdraws or is disqualified midway, all their previous competitions will be canceled and not counted.

16. During the competition, the two participating teams may each send one recorder and one timer to perform their duties together with the staff appointed by this league.

17. If a member has a protest, they should submit a formal protest letter to the secretariat within two days after the incident occurs, and submit it to the committee for judgment. All protests must be accompanied by a deposit of five yuan. If the committee believes that the protest has sufficient grounds, the deposit will be refunded; otherwise, it will be confiscated. The committee's judgment is final and cannot be protested.

18. Teams without uniformed players or players without numbers are not allowed to participate in the competition.

A total of 30,000 tickets have been printed and distributed in advance, all of which have been claimed. Time: starting at 2 PM today. Location: China Football Field on Avenue de l'Observatoire in the French Concession. It is expected that the football field today will be a lively and grand occasion. There are also military bands from the two schools playing music on the field. At the same time, 30,000 copies of the commemorative special issue are printed and presented to the guests.
